German Military Officer Case Adjudicated

Each Sentenced to Eighteen Months Imprisonment

Reuters, Leipzig, 4th – The case against German junior military officers Schlinger, Ruding, and Winde, who were accused of conspiracy to commit treason, was concluded today. The three defendants were each sentenced to eighteen months of imprisonment and ordered to pay court costs. It is reported that Schlinger and Ruding have already been dismissed from their military positions, while Winde resigned voluntarily a year ago. After the case is closed, the three will be detained in a fortress for one year. The time spent in detention awaiting trial will be deducted by six months.

Domestic News

Central Army Advances to Kaifeng

Tickets for Westbound Longhai Line Trains Reach Minquan. News from Xuzhou indicates that the Central Army on the Longhai Line, after capturing the county seat of Lanfeng on the morning of the 30th, continued its westward advance. The right wing, consisting of the troops of Fan Xiji, Ruan Zhaochang, Jin Handing, and others, and the left wing, consisting of the troops of Chiang Ting-wen, Yang Shengzhi, and others, advanced separately. Feng's army had deployed its defenses in eastern Henan, with Lanfeng being the most heavily fortified. With the fall of Lanfeng, Kaifeng was in imminent danger. Today (the 3rd), according to a telegram received by the Transportation Headquarters from the front lines, the Central Army arrived at Kaifeng Railway Station at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 2nd. Feng's troops in the Bian garrison had already retreated westward in droves. Feng's troops in Zhuxianzhen, Chenliu, Tongxu, and Weishi, south of Kaifeng, had been engaged in fierce fighting with the units of the Central Army that had outflanked them from the Pinghan Line. With the retreat, they also withdrew westward. It is observed that Feng's army is urgently transporting troops to Zhengzhou, intending to retreat entirely to Hebei. According to railway sources, the damage to the railway tracks caused by Feng's army's retreat was not extensive. Tickets for westbound Longhai Line trains began reaching Minquan on the 3rd, and military trains reached Lanfeng. Telephone communication extended to Luowang. According to military sources, Feng has expressed his intention to step down, and negotiations are underway for the reorganization of his troops. Commander-in-Chief Chiang has telegraphed Ma Fuxiang and Zhang Zhijiang to the front lines to discuss the resettlement of Feng's troops and the rehabilitation of the Northwest. The Central Army on the Pinghan Line is swiftly flanking Zhengzhou and Luoyang and will likely capture them soon. Qian Zongze previously dispatched the Chief of the Transportation Office, Lü Yunsun, to Wuhan to work with representatives from the Pinghan Railway to handle transportation. Now, Zhang Guohua, the Director of the Office stationed at the front lines, has been dispatched by plane to the Pinghan Line to prepare for military transportation to Zhengzhou. (3rd) Another report states that the Central Army on the Longhai Line occupied Kaifeng Railway Station on the evening of the 2nd. Initially, there was still a portion of Feng's army covering the retreat in Kaifeng city. The various units of the Central Army immediately attacked Bian city. Feng's troops retreated towards Chenqiao in Hebei overnight. The 26th Army of Fan Xiji attacked the northeast gates of Kaifeng from the right wing, while the 2nd Training Division of Zhang Zhizhong attacked the south gate of Kaifeng from the left wing, and they successively entered the city. In this battle, Feng's army retreated hastily and did not have time to destroy the railway lines. One large locomotive and over thirty carriages were abandoned at Kaifeng Station and captured by the Central Army. The units of the Central Army have been advancing westward at full speed. Today (the 4th), according to a telephone call from Lanfeng, the vanguard of the Central Army has passed Zhongmu, reached Baisha, and is advancing rapidly towards Zhengzhou. The railway lines near Kaifeng have not been damaged, and transportation is recovering rapidly. The Railway Bureau has scheduled daily round-trip passenger trains between Xuzhou and Bian starting from the 4th. The passenger train from Xuzhou Station departs westward at 7:30 AM, and the passenger train from Bian Station arrives in Xuzhou at 9:20 PM. However, the telegraph lines to Kaifeng have not yet been repaired. Telegraph communication to Lanfeng was expected to be fully restored by the morning of the 4th. (4th)

Taiyuan's Security and Finance

Widespread Rumors, Tense Financial Situation. Taiyuan Correspondent: The situation in Taiyuan city has recently resembled a martial law zone. Various military, police, and constitutional agencies have dispatched a large number of soldiers to patrol the streets day and night. Rumors are rampant, causing considerable unease among the people. Therefore, the provincial government, the garrison headquarters, and other agencies have issued several announcements, which are visible in every street and alley. The garrison headquarters, citing the imminent arrival of winter and the ease with which petty thieves can operate, also convened a winter defense conference yesterday, attended by military and police agencies. It was decided to establish a joint military, police, and constitutional inspection team at the north and south gates, deploying one lieutenant officer and thirty soldiers to each location to conduct inspections of pedestrians and maintain public order. Furthermore, the district offices of the city have recently, due to the unstable situation and military tensions, held security conferences convened by District Chief Yao of the First District in the meeting room of the district office. It is reported that the outcome of the discussions was that each district will select twenty capable police officers to form a night patrol team, with a patrol officer appointed as the team leader. Firearms are currently being issued, and intensive training is underway. The teams will be formally established and begin patrolling the streets at night soon.

As for the financial situation, it is extraordinarily tense, unprecedented in recent history. Businesses have stopped selling goods, and grain stores are not selling rice or flour. Merchants and wealthy households who hold Jin currency regard it as worthless. The prices of all retail goods in the market change several times a day. On the 19th, a bag of flour cost five yuan and sixty cents. On the 20th, it cost six yuan and forty cents. On the 21st, it had already risen to eight yuan and twenty cents, and there was only a quoted price but no actual goods available. Small-milled flour cost thirteen yuan and fifty cents per hundred catties in the morning of the 19th, fourteen yuan in the afternoon, sixteen yuan on the 20th, and eighteen yuan on the 21st. Similarly, Parisian wool fabric cost nine jiao per foot on the 19th and one yuan and forty jiao on the 20th. The prices of all other goods have increased. Merchants who previously aimed to attract customers now greet them with furrowed brows. As of the 21st, every hundred yuan in silver could be exchanged for two hundred and twenty yuan in paper currency. However, even with paper currency, it is impossible to exchange it for silver. Furthermore, remittances from Taiyuan to other cities have been suspended for several days. The general public feels extremely burdened by the cost of living. As for how the authorities will rectify the situation in the future, no concrete measures have been proposed. The value of all kinds of goods continues to rise sharply.

The Recapture of Yongzhou, Hunan Province: An Account

Tang Shengming and Others Retreat to Quanzhou. Changsha Correspondent: The Gui Clique's Tang Shengming, Yan Renyi, Wang Ge, Feng Tianzhu, and others took advantage of the Communist bandits' attack on Changsha to occupy Yongzhou and advance towards Hengbao. He Jian forced Tang Shengming and others to retreat to Dong'an to await negotiations for their incorporation. Thereupon, the Xiangnan Garrison Commander, Brigade Commander Duan Heng, seized the opportunity to recapture Yongzhou. Unexpectedly, while the incorporation issue was being negotiated, the Gui army again attempted to enter Hunan, and Tang and others reoccupied Yongzhou and invaded Qiyang. Upon hearing this, He Jian immediately telegraphed Duan Heng in secret, instructing him to assemble a superior force as soon as possible, before the main force of the Gui army entered Hunan, and quickly resolve the Tang Shengming and Yan Renyi units. He also ordered the newly appointed Commander of the 16th Division, Peng Weiren, to immediately inspect and direct the defense plan in Baoqing and Qiyang. Duan Heng, upon receiving the order, mobilized more than five regiments on the 28th, dividing them into three routes to attack Yongzhou. (1) The Xiangnan Garrison Commander, commanding the two regiments of Chen Hanxiong and Yu Gongqian, attacked Yongzhou from the front via Qiyang. (2) The 46th Brigade Commander of the 16th Division, Zhang Liangji, commanding the regiment of He Jingcheng, attacked the left wing of Yongzhou via Wenmingpu and Huangyangsi. (3) The Commander of the 3rd Column of the Xiangnan Local Defense, Ou Guan, commanding approximately two regiments of local troops, attacked the right wing of Yongzhou via Ningyuan and Daoxian. At dawn on the 29th, the three routes mobilized simultaneously. Tang, Yan, and others had only about 3,000 troops in the Yongqi area. There were only two brief engagements. On the 29th, the Chen regiment of Duan's command engaged the Yan Renyi unit at Daqiao for about two hours. Yan's unit was unable to withstand the pressure and retreated in disarray towards Yongzhou. On the 30th, the He regiment on the left wing engaged the Tang Shengming unit at Lengshuitan. While they were locked in a stalemate, the Ou Guan unit on the right wing had already occupied Yongzhou's Chaizi Temple. Tang's unit collapsed without a fight and also retreated into Yongzhou city. Thereupon, Duan, Zhang, and Ou's three routes all reached the vicinity of Yongzhou on the evening of the 30th and decided to besiege Yongcheng on the morning of October 1st. At that time, the main force of the Gui army was still in Guilin and Quanzhou and had not yet entered Hunan. Yongzhou only had the Tang, Yan, and other units, who knew they were no match. They abandoned Yongzhou at 10:00 AM on the 1st and retreated towards Quanzhou. Yongzhou was thus recaptured for the second time. The first to enter the city was the Chen Hanxiong regiment directly under Duan Heng's command. Upon receiving the report, Peng Weiren departed from Baoqing on the 2nd and rushed to Yongzhou to direct the suppression and plan the defenses. The telegrams received are recorded as follows: (1) Telegram from Xiangnan Garrison Commander Duan Heng: "My Chen Hanxiong regiment occupied Yongzhou at 10:00 AM on the eastern day. The rebel enemies fled towards Quanzhou and Huangsha River. I have ordered the regiment to pursue and attack. Respectfully submitted, Duan Heng, Seal of Dongwu." (2) Telegram from Daoxian County Magistrate Qu Jun: "At dawn, my local troops pressed towards Wojiashan, attacking the Tang rebels towards Yongzhou. The rebel troops fled towards the Huangsha River area on the previous evening. In addition to ordering the 4th team to enter Yongcheng on the eastern afternoon to maintain order, respectfully submitted, Qu Jun, County Magistrate and Director of Local Troops, Daoxian, Seal of Dong." (3) Telegram from Lingling (i.e., Yongzhou) County Magistrate Wen Daoheng: "On the previous evening, I advanced from Qiyang and stationed myself at Zhengjiaqiao and Wenjiaqiao near Duitangping, gathering and addressing the local troops of the entire county. Morale is very high. I personally led the advance with the army and returned to the county on the eastern day. Details to be submitted later, Wen Daoheng, County Magistrate of Lingling, Dong (October 2nd)."

Sun Tongxuan Stationed in Dezhou to Suppress Bandits

Jinan Correspondent: Sun Tongxuan, Commander of the 12th Army, originally stationed in Pingyuan, commanding military affairs north of the Yellow River, arrived in Dezhou on the 2nd to inspect the 59th Brigade of Zhao Xinde under his command and dispatched two regiments of the brigade to Deping to suppress bandits. It is reported that the local bandits there have gathered over two thousand people and are former troops of Gu Zhenzhi of the 1st Army of the 30th Route Army of the former Jin army. Previously, the General Headquarters dispatched Mei Jun, Commander of the Newly Organized 1st Army, to pacify them. After Sun Tongxuan arrived in Dezhou, he telegraphed Han Fuju, advocating that if the bandits did not submit, they should be suppressed immediately. Today, the provincial government received another emergency telegram, stating that the bandits were besieging Deping. However, it is not yet known whether Zhao's brigade had arrived for suppression. Furthermore, the bandit gang of Cui Jiu, which disturbed the Guangrao area, was previously scattered by the troops of Cao Fulin of the 14th Army. Now, with the army crossing the river, the rear defenses could not be adequately maintained. Cui has regrouped his bandit gang and is now approaching the Zhao and Ai villages two or three li from Guangrao. Upon receiving the report, the General Headquarters has telegraphed Qiao Lizhi of the 74th Division of the Army, ordering him to actively suppress the bandits. After receiving the order, Qiao immediately selected two battalions of Chen's brigade from the division and personally led them to suppress the bandits. Furthermore, the Tiebanhui Society was discovered at the Dalinchi Railway Station on the Jiaoji Railway last month, disturbing the local area. After being suppressed by the army, they fled to the Laiwu area on the 27th of last month, and Dalinchi has been cleared. On the 29th of last month, Zhan Shutang, Commander of the 73rd Division, and Lei Taiping, Commander of the Handgun Brigade, jointly suppressed the bandit gang in Jingzhi Town, Anqiu. The bandits were unable to withstand the pressure and dispersed on the same day, fleeing to the Taqiao area in the southern countryside of Jiaoxian, where there are still seven or eight hundred people. Jiaoxian has telegraphed the province for assistance. According to people from Anqiu, the losses from the bandit robbery in Jingzhi Town amounted to over two million yuan, and over a hundred women were abducted.

In addition, bandit leaders Wang Sitai, Gezi, and Kang, along with three or four hundred men, are rampant in the Jiangluo Town area bordering Linqu and Anqiu. The people in the western countryside of Anqiu have gone to Anqiu to request that Zhan Shutang, Commander of the 73rd Division, send troops to suppress the bandits.

Negotiations on the Arrest of Bandits in the French Concession of Hankou

Hankou Correspondent: Yang Qi, a platoon leader of the 6th Regiment of the 3rd Training Division, responsible for the Wuhan garrison, mistakenly entered the French Concession on the evening of September 26th at 7:00 PM, with two soldiers, while pursuing Zhao Xiuwen, a bandit sent by He Long. The French Consul Botz deemed this an unauthorized action and protested to the garrison headquarters. The headquarters issued a reply to the French Consul on the 3rd, severely refuting the protest. The French Consul's protest and the garrison headquarters' reply are extracted as follows: French Consul's Protest: "To the esteemed Sir, On the 26th of this month, at 7:00 PM, gunshots occurred on Rue Foch in this concession. At the time, a Chinese military officer, identified as Yang Qi, a platoon leader of the 6th Regiment of the 3rd Training Division, accompanied by two soldiers from the 5th Company, pursued a man named Zhao Xiuwen from the Chinese territory. After seeing him enter the concession, they decided to arrest him only after seeing him enter No. 8, Rue Massenet. Zhao, seeing them ascend the stairs and enter the room, jumped out of the window and escaped. Yang Qi and the soldiers fired their guns at the street from the window. After Zhao returned fire, he fled towards Rue de l'Amitie. The above-mentioned circumstances were recounted by Yang Qi to the Chief Inspector of this Concession Police Department after the incident and were confirmed by a joint inspection of the scene of the incident. However, yesterday, several military officers suddenly went to the police department to inquire about Yang Qi's whereabouts. From this, it is evident that he has not yet returned to camp. Moreover, Dr. He, who lives in Rue Massenet, has not returned home since leaving on the 25th. There are many points of suspicion. However, this Consul protests to your esteemed headquarters regarding the unauthorized actions of the Chinese military officer in this concession. If the military officer was indeed pursuing a bandit, he should have reported it to the police department after entering the concession, making it easy to surround and arrest the bandit and avoid the danger of firing guns in the street and injuring innocent pedestrians. This is respectfully submitted. Botz." Garrison Headquarters' Reply: "In reply to your esteemed office's letter of September 29th regarding the case of Yang Qi, a platoon leader of the 6th Regiment of the 3rd Training Division, firing guns and exchanging fire with the bandit Zhao Xiuwen at No. 8, Rue Massenet, after the latter jumped out of the window while being pursued by Yang and two soldiers, apart from the original text being exempted from full transcription, the last two lines of your letter state, 'This Consul protests to your esteemed headquarters regarding the unauthorized actions of the Chinese military officer in this concession. If the military officer was indeed pursuing a bandit, he should have reported it to the police department after entering the concession, making it easy to surround and arrest the bandit and avoid the danger of firing guns in the street and injuring innocent pedestrians.' According to the report from Zhang Dingming, the regimental commander of the regiment, Yang Qi, the platoon leader of the 5th Company, secretly reported that He Long had recently sent bandits to Wuhan to plot an uprising. Zhao Xiuwen was responsible for military guidance. Yang had previously encountered the bandit once and requested that someone be sent to arrest him as soon as possible to prevent the emergence of chaos. The regimental commander, in order to maintain local security and prevent problems before they arose, sent Yang with two soldiers to Hankou to arrest the bandit secretly. It is reported that on the afternoon of the 26th, Yang caught sight of the bandit on the Chinese street and immediately went forward to arrest him. The bandit, fearing punishment, fled into Rue Massenet in the French Concession. Yang and the soldiers either did not know the regulations of the concession or simply did not have time to distinguish which street belonged to the concession and pursued him in a moment of urgency, firing shots from a distance but failing to hit the bandit, allowing him to escape. As for whether Yang and the soldiers have returned to the company, their whereabouts are unknown. It is difficult to predict whether they have been harmed by the bandits. We are currently sending people out to search for them everywhere. It is true that Yang entered the concession to arrest the bandit without reporting to the police department for assistance, which shows a lack of knowledge of the procedures or a failure to distinguish which street belonged to the concession in a moment of urgency, resulting in an error. This was not intentional. In light of the foregoing, we hereby reply to your esteemed office for your information and request that your esteemed Concession Police Department investigate the whereabouts of Yang and report back. To the French Consulate General in Hankou, Commander Xia Douyin. (October 4th)."

Provincial Training Department Sends Personnel to Guide the Organization of People's Groups

Zhenjiang Correspondent: The reorganization of people's groups in various counties of this province is currently underway. However, the progress in various places is very slow. Some are unclear about the meaning of the laws and regulations and do not know how to proceed. Others misunderstand the laws and regulations and proceed illegally. Still others do not follow the organizational procedures for people's groups or violate the guidance of the Party. There are also internal factional disputes within groups, which hinder the progress of reorganization. Various complex situations constantly exceed expectations. The Central Government has high expectations for the reorganization of people's groups in Jiangsu Province. The Provincial Training Department, acting on the instructions of the Central Government, observed the actual situation in various places and realized that it would be difficult to achieve success in reorganizing people's groups without sending personnel to various places to provide on-site guidance. Therefore, it immediately formulated measures for the district-by-district guidance and organization of people's groups, roughly dividing the province into five districts based on the old Circuit system, with slight modifications. Counties with convenient transportation and a slight foundation for the organization of people's groups will be guided first and included in the first phase. Counties with obstructed transportation, many bandits, and no rudimentary form of people's groups will be guided later and included in the second phase. Each phase will last one month, and it is estimated that the work can be completed in about two months. The instructors will be selected from among the capable and experienced staff of the Provincial Reorganization Committee and supplemented by two comrades with experience in mass movements from outside the committee. It is reported that they will depart and begin their work around the Double Tenth Festival.

Famous people will be invited to give speeches, and experts will be invited to perform new anti-drug dramas and show recent films of anti-drug activities in Shanxi. Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Details of a Murder for Money Case: In the 359th Tu area outside Dazhangjing, several individuals resembling roaming soldiers were strolling and playing on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. Villagers were working in the fields when they suddenly saw these people producing bamboo spears. One person was stabbed and suffered a severe wound, collapsing to the ground and rolling around. The others had already scattered. The villagers reported the incident to the military and police authorities, who sent people to the scene. The injured person was on the verge of death but was still able to say that he had been stabbed to death by his own gang. Unexpectedly, the next day, someone resembling his companion sought revenge from the villagers there, falsely accusing the deceased of being stabbed to death by the villagers and tying up and beating Wang Adong and Zhuo Fu. The court then conducted an autopsy and burial. A certain agency, in accordance with the deceased's last words, arrested one of the criminals and found eighty yuan in banknotes. It was learned that this was a case of accomplices murdering for money, luring the victim to the countryside and attacking him. However, the villagers there not only suffered fear and panic but also had their miscellaneous items destroyed, resulting in losses. The victims have reported the matter to the court for investigation. Wang Adong and the other two will also be questioned and released by the court.

Suzhou

Zhang Minggao Arrested and Escorted to Suzhou: This spring, when Hu Zuyu concurrently served as the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Taihu Lake, Zhang Minggao, the Chief of the Changxing Security Group in Zhejiang, was ordered to set out to suppress bandits but instead took his troops and weapons and surrendered to the bandits in Taihu Lake. The Zhejiang Provincial Government issued an arrest warrant with a reward of two thousand yuan. The 3rd District of the Suzhou Public Security Bureau received this cooperative arrest document. The Detective Team Leader Xu Fengshan paid close attention to the matter. The day before yesterday (the 4th) at 8:00 PM, Detective Yang Shangkang learned in Shanghai that Zhang was recently hiding at No. 12, Youqing Lane, opposite the Great World in Shanghai. He immediately went to the address with Patrol Officer Hu Xianzhang of this district, along with Detective Shen Jinshu of the French Police Department and West Section Chief Baurder, and arrested Zhang. Zhang initially claimed that his surname was Chen and that he was acquainted with a certain shoe store at the intersection of the Great Road. However, he was identified as Zhang Minggao and was taken to the headquarters of the 3rd District of the Public Security Bureau in Suzhou at 2:00 AM yesterday (the 5th) for temporary detention, pending his transfer to Zhejiang Province for interrogation.

Request to Send Personnel to Resolve the Xuanmiao Temple Screen Wall Issue: Regarding the case of reconstructing the screen wall and three gates of Suzhou's Xuanmiao Temple into a commercial market, the preservationists advocate preserving the historical site and not allowing reconstruction, while the pro-business faction advocates demolishing and rebuilding the stores. Both sides have submitted requests to the ministries, academies, provinces, and departments, and the case has been pending for two months without resolution. The National Goods Relief Association here has also submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, stating that if the three gates are rebuilt into a commercial market, a national goods commercial market should be established to promote national goods. Yesterday, the ministry approved an order from the Executive Yuan, stating that the demolition of Suzhou's Xuanmiao Temple has been ordered by the National Government to be stopped immediately by the Jiangsu Provincial Government and instructed to hand over the matter to the provincial government for immediate stoppage of the demolition and to the Ministry of the Interior for thorough investigation and appropriate handling. It is noted that Suzhou's Xuanmiao Temple, as a historical site, should be preserved. Since the demolition has been ordered to be stopped, the request of the association to reconstruct the three gates of the temple to establish a national goods store should be discussed. In addition to submitting a reply, we must also comply with the regulations. The Wu County Party Headquarters yesterday specifically submitted a report to the Provincial Party Headquarters, which was forwarded to the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government, instructing the various ministries, academies, and departments to send personnel to Suzhou to jointly inspect and discuss the matter with the Party and government agencies in order to seek a final resolution.

Wuxi

Unsuccessful Mediation of a Kerosene Storage Dispute: Ge Zicai, the manager of the Yuanda Company in this county, purchased land outside the East Gate in Yangli Lane to build a kerosene storage tank. Nearby residents and silk factories strongly opposed it, fearing immediate explosions and the potential harm to life and property from any sparks falling from the kerosene tank. Both sides held extreme positions. Yesterday, the county government convened both parties for reconciliation. Attendees included Yuanda's manager Ge Zicai, residents' representative Sheng Zhuofu, silk factories’ representative Chen Tongfu and over ten others. Cheng Jingtang, the executive member of the County Chamber of Commerce, also attended the meeting. Section Chief Wei represented the chair, suggesting that both parties compromise to maintain harmony. However, after two hours of debate without resolution, it was decided that Cheng Jingtang would act as a mediator in his private capacity. If still unresolved, the matter will be submitted to the Construction Department for personnel to be sent to Wuxi for handling.

Police Sub-bureau Chief Accused of Assault: Zhou Yangzhao, the chief of the Fifth Police Sub-bureau outside the North Gate in Jiangyin Lane, has been criticized for poor performance since taking office, leading to complaints filed to the provincial government by local residents. Zhou Yangzhao suspected that Li Jie, a resident of Hou Qi Lane, orchestrated these complaints, harboring deep resentment. Ruan Renqing, an investigating officer in the sub-bureau, also resented Li Jie for failing to secure a loan and sought revenge. Recently, Zhou Yangzhao, along with Investigator Ruan Renqing, several police officers, and local thug Feng Licheng, searched Li Jie's home in Hou Qi Lane under the pretext of inspecting prohibited items. Finding nothing, they tied Li Jie's hands and brutally beat him with a leather whip, causing injuries all over his body. Li Jie filed a complaint with the county government yesterday, accusing Zhou Yangzhao and others of abusing their power for personal revenge and assault, requesting Zhou Yangzhao and Ruan Renqing to be summoned for legal investigation.

Strict Punishment for Illicit Production of Inferior Silkworm Eggs: Wang Songcheng, director of the sericulture guidance center in Xingtan Town, Huai Xia (Eighth District), and Deputy Town Head Fan Luweng, discovered that Zhu Xiangguan, a villager from Jialong Bridge in the town, was privately producing inferior silkworm eggs, harming the local community. They reported to the district security corps, who sent police to investigate and arrest Zhu. They seized three carrying poles of inferior silkworm eggs and seventy-one blue lead pupal rings, along with one hundred and fifty-nine pieces of Jiangzhen Shuixing breeding farm cardboard. These were all sent to the Sixteenth Police Sub-bureau, then to the County Public Security Bureau. Director Xu interrogated Zhu Xiangguan, who confessed that Fan Hanwen manufactured the inferior eggs and related equipment, and that he only provided the money to purchase the silkworm larvae. Director Xu, recognizing the severe harm caused by the proliferation of inferior silkworm eggs, ordered strict handling and immediately prepared a document for submission to the county government for judicial proceedings.

Petition to Protect Taihu Lake Scenery: Hua Yinchun, an inspector from the Agricultural and Mining Department, recently noted that hills around Taihu Lake, such as the Southern Dushan, Ludingshan, Chongshan, Baojieshan, Qitangshan, Guanshan, Yeshan, Longwangshan, Jiantingshan, Xusheshan, and Laohushan around Wulihu, are being privately quarried for stones. Only the Sheshan, Daji, and Dajishan hills have not been exploited. The azure mountains and lake are not only turning into barren hills but also becoming red cliffs, utterly ruining the scenery. He submitted a detailed map and requested the Agricultural and Mining Department to strictly prohibit quarrying. Minister He, based on the report, ordered the county government yesterday to strictly enforce the ban, investigate and identify the quarrying locations and responsible parties, and order them to cease work, in accordance with Articles 94 and 97 of the Mining Regulations to protect the lake scenery.

Changzhou

Inspecting Magistrate Goes to Baizhang to Examine Corpse: The Baizhang Town Security Corps in the Fourth District of Wuyi County was surrounded and disarmed by police and security from Jiangyin, mistakenly shooting and beheading Peng Quanlin, the younger brother of Peng Jinkang, the head of Changchun Township. The Fourth District Head Cheng Foyu reported this to the County Court for examination. The Inspecting Magistrate led officials to Baizhang on the morning of the 4th, first summoning the deceased’s wife, Peng Ding, for questioning. Peng Ding tearfully recounted how her husband was shot and beheaded and repeatedly pleaded for justice. The magistrate then conducted an autopsy, confirming that the deceased was shot and beheaded while alive. The magistrate ordered the deceased’s brother to prepare the funeral arrangements. Since the incident, all stores in the town have been closed. The Inspecting Magistrate went to each store to persuade them, promising to investigate the truth and severely punish the perpetrators. The stores then gradually reopened.

Robbery Occurs Near Mahang Bridge: Ma Genxi's house in Daxhang Shang near Mahang Bridge, Wuyi County, was suddenly attacked by many bandits around 3 AM on the 4th. They tied up Ma Genxi's mother, wife, and daughter, then looted their property. Before leaving, they locked the front door. The next morning, neighbors, noticing no activity at Ma's house, forced their way inside and found the three still tied up on the ground. Upon learning what happened, they freed them. The reported loss was about one or two hundred yuan.

Jiangyin

Chen Mengxing Summoned for County Interrogation: Chen Mengxing, the former head of the Seventh District, was previously accused to the Civilian Department of bribing Fang Debiao, a bandit, by Xu Xiaochuan, the captain of the first police unit. Now Chen Mengxing was accused of opium smoking. Yesterday afternoon, he was summoned by the Public Security Bureau to the county. After interrogation by County Magistrate Li, Chen admitted to making the accusations but denied smoking opium. He was detained for further investigation.

Unexpected Twist in Ji Hehua Case: Ji Hehua, the former director of the Municipal Administration Bureau, was detained and interrogated for counter-revolutionary activities. His father, Ji Ziqing, offered three thousand yuan to the county to purchase guns for the self-defense corps, which was rejected. Previously reported. Recently, his father, Ji Ziqing, and mother, Ji Sha, gave five thousand yuan to the former director of the Relief Institute, Jiang Hong, for the Relief Institute and the purchase of guns. County Magistrate Li learned of this and summoned Ji Sha and Jiang Hong to the court on the afternoon of the 4th, and questioned Ji Hehua. Ji Sha confessed that she gave the money to Jiang Hong to rescue her son. Jiang Hong said that he received five thousand yuan, including one thousand yuan in Chengfeng Village notes, three thousand yuan in bank passbooks, and one thousand yuan given to Chen Zhongda, the property manager, for safekeeping. County Magistrate Li was furious that Jiang Hong used the county government's name to accept large sums of money, an act of bribery. He ordered Jiang Hong to be detained in prison for investigation, Ji Hehua to be returned to custody, and Ji Sha to be released on bail. He ordered clerk Cui Xilin to investigate at Yongcheng Village, confirming that Hongji received 500 yuan on October 2nd and 500 yuan on the 4th, paying out 100 yuan on the same day, leaving 900 yuan in the village's custody. He also investigated at Chengfeng Village, confirming that under the name of Gongji on September 21st, 2,000 yuan in foreign currency were dated October 11th, with 1,000 yuan to Gongliji and 2,000 yuan to Gongliji in the same period. 2,000 yuan were paid to Gongliji on October 2nd, leaving 3,000 yuan to be kept by the village under the name of Gongji.

Zhenjiang

Civil Affairs Department Sets Deadline for Supervising the Compilation of Security Corps: After the establishment of the Provincial Capital Guard Zone, the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department, in accordance with the Provincial Government's resolution, jointly appointed Wang Lanqing with the Jiangsu Provincial Security Office as a special commissioner to supervise the compilation of the Security Corps in the Provincial Capital Guard Zone. Bandits frequently harassed the six counties in the guard zone, necessitating the completion of the Security Corps' compilation as soon as possible to provide adequate defense. Therefore, yesterday, the department specifically instructed the commissioner to immediately travel to Danyang, Yangzhong, Zhenjiang, Jiangdu, Yizheng, and Jurong counties to work with the county magistrates, to complete the supervision of the Security Corps' compilation within one month. The department also ordered to brand and register all civilian-owned firearms within their jurisdiction, and those who conceal such weapons will be punished as possessing illegal military supplies upon discovery. The department also ordered each county magistrate to prepare to receive the commissioner for inspection.

Gao Zhongkui and Others Regain Freedom: Gao Zhongkui, the Third Brigade Commander of the Provisional 14th Division of the Army, and Deputy Brigade Commander Yin Bochun, were ordered to go to Shandong for defense. While passing through Qingjiang, they were mistakenly detained by the 266th Regiment and transferred to the Brigade Headquarters in Yangzhou. Yesterday, they were transferred to the province where the Security Office investigated and found it to be a misunderstanding, and they were immediately released and regained their freedom. Commander Gao has now gone to Beijing and is en route to the front lines.

Adjutant Liu's Home Robbed: The home of Adjutant Hua Ziyan, located east of Wanshou Temple behind Shengyun Nunnery, was robbed on the night of the 2nd by several plainclothes bandits. Huzhou

Colluding with External Bandits to Kidnap Relatives: In Jin Sheng, in the Guxia Village area north of Heping, Changxing, Zhejiang, all the residents are surnamed Yin. One Yin Zilong, known for his unprincipled behavior, has been associating with bandits recently. In February of this year, he gathered external bandits to kidnap his relative Yin Lisheng, who was ransomed for five hundred yuan. Yin Zilong's house often has suspicious guests coming and going, and his wife, Wu, diligently provides hospitality, with irregular meals and lodging. This was later discovered by villagers, leading to some gossip, which angered Yin Zilong and his wife. This led to arson, with several houses belonging to Yin Jinyuan, Yin Changbao, Chen Jinsheng, and others being burned to the ground. On the 14th of last month, Yin Zilong even dared to lead more than ten guest bandits, each carrying guns, to rob the houses of Yin Fuqing, Yin Achuan, and others. Because the villagers feared his violence, they dared not report it. However, this was discovered by Squad Leader Xu of the security team stationed in Xiaoshi. Bandits Rob Rice: In the Sanguanmiao area near Gangkou Town, Changxing, a farmer surnamed Wang from Henan rented over one hundred acres of land. He had stored over one hundred dan of harvested rice at home. However, on the night of the 2nd of this month, three bandit boats suddenly arrived with over twenty bandits, who stole all of Wang's stored rice.

Hangzhou Rice Prices Plunge Again: In Hangzhou, due to the arrival of new grain and a large number of boats, top-quality rice prices have fallen from eighteen yuan to thirteen yuan. Xiaoshan

Another Robbery Case in Laohu Township: Robberies have been occurring frequently in Xiaoshan's urban and rural areas lately without any solved, leading to a further increase in theft. It is now known that in Laohu Township, about ten li from the East Gate, the home of Zhang Peigao was robbed by over twenty bandits around 10 PM last night (the 2nd). They carried blades and electric torches and used long bamboo poles to enter over the wall. Zhang's entire family knew about the bandits and had fled, but the housewife was tied up and forced to reveal the hiding place of valuables. They looted for about an hour before opening the door and escaping. After inspection, it was discovered that over six hundred yuan in silver dollars, over two hundred yuan in silver coins, pearls, gold and silver items, and leather clothes were stolen, with losses exceeding three thousand yuan.

County Court President Transferred to Provincial Appointment: Yang Ti, the President of the Xiaoshan County Court, has been in office for almost a year. He has now received instructions from the High Court to be transferred to the province for another appointment. It is reported that Wu has been appointed to fill the vacancy. After receiving the order, Yang ordered his staff to expedite the completion of their work. Once the new appointee arrives in Xiaoshan, he will hand over the office and depart.

Shangyu

Luo Futai's Home Robbed: Huangni, Qianjiang, and Pilian Hutian near Baiguan are close to Houhai. Luo Futai, a resident of the village, used to trade in Hanyang but has now retreated to farming and is moderately wealthy. Bandits coveted his wealth. At about 10 PM at the end of last month, eight or nine bandits in short clothes and carrying weapons suddenly broke through the door and entered, first driving Luo and his family into a room, guarded by a bandit outside, and then ransacking the upstairs. As a result, over one hundred yuan in silver, three to four hundred yuan in soft jewelry, and several silk clothes drying downstairs were all robbed. Because Luo's residence was remote, no neighbors heard anything when the bandits entered, allowing them to plunder to their heart's content.

Special Report

Opinion Paper on Revenue Policy by the Ministry of Finance Gammer and Other Design Committee (3rd continuation)

The plan for a consumption tax system should first clarify the interrelationship between tariffs and inland taxes, or rejected taxes. Import tariffs should not be increased excessively, causing capital and labor to flow from industries that naturally profit to industries that artificially profit due to higher prices of foreign goods, thereby increasing the prices of domestic goods. This will have an adverse impact on national finances. On one hand, revenue from import tariffs will decrease significantly; on the other hand, artificially raising the price of certain goods through manpower will cause capital and labor to leave the industries they have traditionally engaged in, thereby greatly reducing the productivity and taxpaying ability of these industries. Therefore, when imposing import taxes on imported goods, a corresponding amount of consumption tax should be levied on domestically produced goods of the same kind. Conversely, when imposing a consumption tax on domestically produced goods, a corresponding import tax should be levied on foreign goods of the same kind; otherwise, the influx of foreign goods will inevitably overwhelm domestic products and greatly harm national finances. Therefore, this committee recommends that the match tax and cement tax apply not only to domestic products but also to foreign goods.

Among the various consumption taxes levied in China, the most notable are the tobacco and alcohol taxes. The taxes levied on cigars and cigarettes do not significantly differ from this committee's opinions on commodity taxes. These opinions have been explained in the aforementioned two drafts. Other tobacco taxes should be carefully considered and revised. Although this committee does not have detailed recommendations on this point, it is reasonable to combine all tobacco and alcohol taxes into one tax. License fees should ideally be incorporated into general business licenses or business taxes. However, since these taxes have been delegated to the provinces, the best solution requires more thorough consideration.

Alcohol tax should be levied on both foreign and domestic goods. Import alcohol taxes should be levied according to a certain tax rate, with customs acting as the collecting agency. The tax rate can be slightly higher than the current prevailing rate. For foreign alcohol produced domestically, a corresponding tax should be levied based on the quality of the alcohol. These taxes and native alcohol taxes should be regarded as inland taxes.

Combining the Tobacco and Alcohol Affairs Bureau with the Rolled Tobacco Consolidated Tax Office will undoubtedly improve the efficiency of tobacco and alcohol tax administration and save administrative costs.

Administrative Organization: This committee has discussed inland tax administration in other reports. What should be reiterated here is that the tax administration of all inland taxes other than salt tax should be consolidated under one office or bureau.

Salt tax is the oldest source of revenue in China, but due to political instability in recent years, its administrative problems differ from those of other taxes. Therefore, the aforementioned plan to consolidate inland taxes under one agency should exclude the Salt Inspectorate. However, this committee's rationale for the draft of the special consumption tax law on matches, submitted on September 6, 1929, strongly advocates for the establishment of a unified agency, called a bureau, office, or agency (the name is irrelevant), directly under the Minister of Finance, to administer all other new and old inland taxes, including the following: rolled tobacco consolidated tax, tobacco and alcohol tax, stamp tax, and special consumption taxes, including the match tax and cement tax recommended by this committee.

The system of various ministries and agencies of the central government independently levying taxes should also be studied. Currently, many agencies outside the Ministry of Finance freely levy taxes under the guise of inspection fees or other names. Although government agencies collecting public fees for their duties should not be considered a loss of natural tax revenue administration, without a single agency handling it, confusion and duplication are inevitable.

This committee has suggested in other drafts that the administration and collection of taxes should be separated and handled by two separate agencies. Strictly supervise the collection of taxes, and all tax revenues should be deposited in the name of the national treasury. If this method can be implemented, the previous system of collecting agencies retaining part of the tax revenue to cover collection costs and only remitting the remaining portion to the national treasury can be abolished. All collection costs should be supervised by the central government and paid directly by the national treasury. Furthermore, after the adoption of this method, all contract donation systems will cease to exist because this system can only exist in improper government organizations. The elimination of the above two systems is undoubtedly necessary.

Finally, there is one important issue that urgently needs to be resolved, namely the division of revenue sources between the central government and local governments. The recommendations for the standards for dividing central tax revenue and local tax revenue (revised based on the recommendations of the National Economic Conference) seem to provide a satisfactory solution to this problem, but the solution should first revise the current tax laws and regulations and reorganize the administrative scope of the central and local governments regarding tax revenue, allowing each to handle its financial resources within its legal scope. This issue is of course related to politics. In short, the division of tax administrative scope is a prerequisite for effective tax administration, and the funds obtained from taxation should be allocated by the central government to local governments level by level, rather than by local governments to the central government. Otherwise, the survival of the central government will depend solely on local governments. (End)

Important Educational News

Ministry of Education Clarifies Membership Qualifications of Educational Associations

The Ministry of Education, based on a report from the Anhui Education Department regarding a telegram from the Lai'an County Education Association requesting clarification of membership qualifications, stated that educational associations are social education organizations. The current committee members and staff who have qualifications of a middle school graduate, if they meet the qualifications in Article 6, Section 1, Paragraph 2 of the Education Association Regulations during the next election, can they be listed as de facto members? The Ministry requests clarification and instructions. The Department states that clarifying legal provisions is not within the Department's jurisdiction, so they are submitting the report for review and clarification. The Ministry recently instructed the Department to reply, stating that Article 6, Section 1, Paragraph 2 of the Education Association Regulations refers to public social education organizations such as public libraries and popular schools that actually implement social education. Educational associations themselves are educational research groups and not educational implementation organizations. Their current committee members and staff cannot obtain the qualifications of de facto members based on the provisions of this article. This should be noted and conveyed for notification.

Ambassadors and Consuls Should Encourage Overseas Chinese to Study Party Doctrine and Native Language

The National Government, based on a report from the Beijing Municipal Party Headquarters requesting that the overseas Party Headquarters at all levels and the ambassadors and consuls abroad be ordered to effectively encourage overseas Chinese to study Party doctrine and native language, has transferred the case to the Ministry of Education for handling. The Ministry of Education has consulted the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for drafting to jointly issue an order.

Correction of Resolutions on Foreigners Coming to China to Investigate Science

The situations regarding the joint meeting of the Central Research Institute and the Ministries of Interior, Foreign Affairs, Military Affairs, Political Affairs, and Education regarding foreigners coming to China to investigate science have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Now the Ministry of Education announced that one item in the meeting minutes should be added with the words "by the competent authority," that is, Article 6, Section 2 of the resolution on the management of Smith et al. carrying weapons into the Yunnan and Guizhou provinces for investigation should be "After the team signs all the conditions, the Provincial Governments of Yunnan and Guizhou will be consulted by the competent authority for verification before entry."

Local News

City Boy Scout Council Election Meeting

｜Eight Directors Elected｜Scheduled Swearing-In Ceremony

The Shanghai City Boy Scout Council held its election meeting yesterday, convened by the Training Department of the City Party Headquarters at the City Party Headquarters. Many service members, representatives from the City Executive Committee, and representatives from the China Boy Scout Headquarters, totaling over a hundred people, attended. The meeting was chaired by Mr. Tong Xingbai, the Training Minister of the City, and the proceedings were as follows:

Chairman's Address: Gentlemen, today we are electing members to the City Boy Scout Council. A total of forty-six people have arrived, and there are ninety-four qualified service members in total. Apart from the five who have asked for leave, there are still eighty-five. The number of people who have arrived today, forty-six, is more than half, so we can officially start the meeting. We know that the Boy Scout cause is both a national and a social cause because Boy Scouts are the nation's most outstanding young citizens and also the fundamental elements in improving society. Therefore, the Boy Scout cause is more important than ordinary national and social causes, and the training of Boy Scouts must be given special attention. During the era of warlord governments, the Boy Scout cause relied on the enthusiasm and efforts of individuals to barely maintain itself. The government paid no attention to it, so the various aspects of the Boy Scouts were very disorganized. Now that our Party is in power, all facilities are based on the Three Principles of the People as the guiding principle of education. The same is true for Boy Scouts. We must ensure that Boy Scout education does not deviate from the educational policy under Party rule and that the Boy Scout cause becomes a truly national and social education center. Shanghai is the most important region in the country. No matter what organization, it needs a central organization to function properly. The same is true for Boy Scouts. If there is no central organization, it is no different from a soulless body. If we want future development, that is just a dream. Therefore, the establishment of the Council is tantamount to creating a new life for the Shanghai Boy Scout cause. Now, with the enthusiastic hope of the Party and the government, and with the sincere request of the Boy Scouts in our city, the Shanghai Council has been successfully established. I believe that after the birth of this group that is tied to a new life, all facilities and all plans can proceed in an orderly and gradual manner. The future development will be forward, and the future of the Shanghai Boy Scout cause will be bright and limitless. I hope that in the future, the members of our city can be more united and consistent, sacrifice personal opinions, and seek a concrete expression of love and sincerity. Finally, I also hope that the future Council will pay attention to (1) the issue of rectifying discipline. We know that discipline is the lifeblood of a group. Without discipline, this group will be scattered. Boy Scouts have the important responsibility of strengthening the nation and transforming society, so they should strictly abide by discipline. (2) Fully develop the spirit of Boy Scouts. The spirit of Boy Scouts is not about the beauty of the style or the spirit of the uniform, but about being able to consistently express the spirit of Boy Scouts in all aspects of work and to promote the virtue of selflessness at all times and in all places, as a model for society and a role model for young people. I deeply hope that you can understand these points and put them into practice.

Preparatory Process: Mr. Zhu Jiarang reported on the preparatory process of the Council, saying that in the past few years, Shanghai Boy Scouts have been very disorganized due to the lack of guiding principles for education. Since our Party came to power, it has greatly reformed the old and bad places, and the same is true for Boy Scouts. Therefore, under the leadership of our Party, the Boy Scout cause is changing and improving day by day. Therefore, the original Boy Scout guidance organizations in Shanghai, such as the Promotion Association, etc., must also be changed. The central government has had many plans and new facilities for the Boy Scout cause. The City Party Headquarters has also followed the instructions of the central government and has had considerable influence. The establishment of the Council today is the result of our influence. The City Party Headquarters has been preparing for the City Council for three months. During this period, because the headquarters has not yet fully established a unified guidance organization, for example, after the proposal of a division-level organization, it was renamed the Council, and at the same time, various regulations have not been promulgated, so it was once suspended during the summer vacation, which is why it has been delayed until now and the City Council has not been established. The first difficulty in establishing the Council is the issue of funding. If there is no funding, it will be difficult to do things. The Director of the City Education Bureau is a natural reason. We contacted him to request a monthly subsidy of 200 yuan, which was finally resolved satisfactorily. This problem has been broken. The second is the issue of the venue. The conditions we require for the venue are: first, the location should be good, second, it should not cost money, and third, the transportation should be convenient. This is very difficult. At first, we wanted to attach it to the City Chamber of Commerce, but because the City Chamber of Commerce has too many affiliated organizations, it was changed to a district party headquarters. However, the transportation of a district party headquarters is inconvenient, but it is better than nothing until we find a suitable place.

Representative's Address: The representative of the China Boy Scout Headquarters said, "Chairman Zhu and Comrade have already reported in detail. I am just here to state a few important hopes of the central government for the Shanghai Council. The Shanghai City Training Department has painstakingly prepared for the establishment of the Council. How should we work hard? How should we think about the future of the Shanghai Boy Scouts so as not to fail their hard work? The organization of the China Boy Scouts is divided into four levels: the national and city/county councils, the provincial council, and the central headquarters. Because the Council has not been established, many barriers have arisen between the central government and the groups. This is because the spatial distance is too far, so the situation is unclear. With the organization of the Council, it will help the headquarters and naturally provide many conveniences to the groups. Therefore, the establishment of the Council is very important. After the establishment of the Council, there will be many conveniences in terms of the organization and assessment of the Boy Scouts. How? Because the central government often cannot take care of the talents of the group leaders, there are often shortcomings. With the organization of the Council, this problem can be easily solved. I hope that after the establishment of the Shanghai Council, we will do our best to do the above things."

Election Results: The winners were Shen Yu, Qu Yue, Wang Gang, Huang Xian, Zhang Xunfang (above are the official directors), Gu Meilai, Zhao Weizu, Wang Wenhua (above are the alternate directors). It is said that the above new directors will be reported to the headquarters for approval by the supervisors and the City Training Department today. The date of the swearing-in ceremony is around the Double Tenth Festival.

Councilors' Talk: After the meeting, the new directors were called together for a talk by Mr. Luo Qiu, the representative of the Boy Scout Headquarters. The City Training Department provided refreshments. Mr. Luo gave detailed instructions on the future direction of the Council.

Grass Tennis Singles A Record

Mr. Hyoro Wins the Championship

｜Qiu Feihai Loses Unluckily Three to One｜

Excellent Ball Skills. Mr. Hyoro, the 1925 All-Japan Singles Champion, defeated our country's Qiu Feihai by a score of three to one and won the Shanghai Grass Tennis Singles Championship. Mr. Hyoro was already leading by two to one the day before, but the game was suspended due to darkness. Yesterday afternoon, the two continued to compete at the French Concession General Assembly. Mr. Hyoro won the fourth set again with six to four, and the victory was completed. The Singles Certificate Championship this year belongs to him. After the game, Mr. White, the president of the Grass Tennis Association, gave a speech and invited Mrs. Donner to give the award and then dispersed.

Qiu Feihai Full of Vigor

The bell rang three times, and the war began. Qiu Feihai was full of vigor and tried to make progress, frequently shooting backhand shots at the opponent, which was quite dominant. He also used the method of feinting to score points many times and won the first game of the fourth set. The second game was wonderful for both of them. A point must be obtained after a lot of hard work and countless struggles, and the difficulty can be imagined. Qiu made great progress in this game, his shots were agile, and his attack was effective. He finally won the game with ten to eight. In the third game, Mr. Hyoro's anger rose, and there were frequent discoveries of touching the net and wild balls. Qiu Feihai was calm and composed and won the third game again. The momentum at that time made it easy to defeat the fourth set and fight Mr. Hyoro to the end.

Mr. Hyoro Wins the Championship After Hard Fighting

However, Mr. Hyoro has been in the battlefield for a long time and has rich experience. Under this difficult situation, he can still act cautiously, which is commendable. He used Qiu's weak serve and suddenly launched a smash, causing Qiu to not be able to look back in time. Because of this, he regained two games, and then used his own serve to gain momentum and won two more games. After twenty minutes, he heard the changes of vicissitudes. It turned out that Mr. Hyoro had already taken the lead and had a score of four to three, and became a trend of turning defeat into victory. Qiu made a great effort to whip, left draw and right hit, and also fought back a game, making the score four to four. In the last two games, the God of Happiness abandoned Qiu and went to Mr. Hyoro, so soon Mr. Hyoro won consecutive victories and won the fourth set with six to four.

Chinese Men's and Women's Singles Championship

Male... Guo Qida

Male... Yang Ren

The Shanghai Open Chinese Singles Championship finals were held yesterday. The participants were Guo Qida and Liu Keng in the men's group, and Yang Ren and Yang Bizhen in the women's group. As a result, Guo Qida won the men's group championship, with a score of three to zero. Yang Ren won the women's group championship, with a score of two to zero.

(1) Men's Group... Guo Qida Wins Liu Keng ｜Three to Zero｜

Guo Qida is good at both offense and defense. His victory in the championship was expected by the audience. As a result, he won in straight sets.

At the beginning of the first set, Liu was repeatedly frustrated and lost three games in a row. It was not until the fourth game that he defeated Guo with four to two. He then lost three games in a row. Guo won the first set with six to one.

In the second set, Liu was fierce at the beginning, his smash was wonderful, and he won with four to one. However, time is no more, Guo then went smoothly and won six games in a row, and became six to one again.

In the third set, Guo still won with six to one. Only in the sixth game, Liu was greatly attacked and ate a slippery four. Liu's performance in that game was very good. In summary, in the three sets, Guo Qida made a uniform color, all with a score of six to one, which is extremely wonderful.

(2) Women's Group... Yang Ren Wins Yang Bizhen

｜Two to Zero｜

Both ladies did not work hard for the qualification for the finals because the other side waived the right in the previous preliminary round, which was cheaper for them. The finals were held yesterday to determine who would win the championship. Both sides have quite strong skills, but Miss Yang Ren's serve is better, and she is willing to work hard to save the ball. Miss Bizhen is not like that. If the opponent's ball is slightly difficult, she will stare blankly and not move her lotus steps easily. The reason for her failure is mostly here. However, sometimes Miss Yang Ren makes some mistakes and often commits suicide. As a result, Miss Yang Ren won the championship with two to zero.

In the first set, a total of ten games were fought in this set. Yang Ren won the first, second, fourth, fifth, sixth, and tenth games, a total of six games. Miss Bizhen won the third, seventh, eighth, and ninth games, a total of four games. Yang Ren won with a score of six to four.

In the second set, Yang Ren won the first, second, third, fifth, sixth, and seventh games, a total of six games. The remaining fourth and eighth games were won by Miss Bizhen. As a result, Miss Yang Ren still won the second set with six to one, and won the women's group championship.
