Free Talk

One Word of Wisdom

— Holding Buddha

Life is like playing cards. Getting good cards is like being born into a wealthy family. Getting bad cards is like being a poor child. Building a family from scratch is like exhausting your efforts. Maybe you can win a big hand, but it is very difficult. It's like someone can give you a card to eat. This is like someone promoting you, so you won't lose money. If your card style is bad and the upper family is desperately trying to nail you, this is like kicking someone when they are down. It's very similar. Like a nouveau riche family, rich people who make money improperly, this is very similar to winning a big hand with active hands.

The human body is the same as heaven and earth. Heaven wants it to be clear and light, and earth wants it to be heavy and turbid. People do not know the way to maintain health. Thinking hurts the brain, and lust hurts the kidneys. The head is not clear, light, heavy, and turbid. The abdomen is not heavy, turbid, clear, and light. The top is heavy and the bottom is light. The center of gravity is lost. As a result, diseases such as headache, dizziness, blurred vision, tinnitus, asthma, kidney deficiency, and nocturnal emission occur. Therefore, the horse stance of martial artists and the dantian breathing of meditators are all paying attention to the way of the top being clear and light and the bottom being heavy and turbid.

Life is thorough. The appearance is empty. It's a pity that many people can't see through it and can't figure it out. Why bother with a narrow mind, arrogant intentions, vanity, and snobbery to build a fence at the bottom of the sea? In my opinion, reading is the most enjoyable and doing good is the most enjoyable.

When people reach middle age, joy is faint. As Wang Dun'gen said, "Even if you play cards with a 10,000-yuan stake today and win a big victory, it is not as fun as playing money sparrow with my late father when I was a child." Alas, the years cannot flow backwards, and if you don't establish a career in this world, how can you not follow Dong E's sigh?

A Brief Note on Fan Diwen's Speech

— Cheng Zhizheng

Former Foreign Minister and Chairman of the Second International, Mr. Fan Diwen, was invited by the Academia Sinica to give a speech in China. He first went to Beiping and Shenyang, and then toured Beijing and Hangzhou. Due to the urgent time, he stayed in Shanghai for only two or three days. Jiaotong University in this city believed that Mr. Fan was the old friend of the Premier and was very clear about the political situation in China, so it specially invited him to the school. Mr. Meng kindly agreed and gave a speech in the Wen Zhi Hall of the school one afternoon. There were no less than a thousand listeners. Among the guests were Mr. Cai Jiemin, the president of the Academia Sinica, and many Westerners. Here are some miscellaneous notes to send to this talk.

Mr. Fan's Appearance: At four o'clock, Mr. Fan and other dignitaries took their seats. Mr. Fan is nearly sixty years old. He has a lot of beard and wears glasses on his nose. His appearance is extraordinary and his spirit is especially bright. First, Li Zhaohuan, the vice minister of the Ministry of Railways and the president of the school, gave a welcome speech, saying that the relationship between China and Belgium is very deep. Mr. Fan advocates national self-determination and world peace, which is especially desired by the Chinese people. Then he translated it into English.

Speaking Entirely in French: Then Mr. Fan gave a speech. At first, I thought it would be in English, but from beginning to end, it was entirely in French. Few people in the audience are proficient in this way, so they can only speculate on its intentions based on its posture. The person standing next to Mr. Li was his full-time translator. Although Mr. Fan's words were incomprehensible, his tone and posture are worthy of being a great orator. At the climax, the voice was like a Hong Zhong, shaking the house. It is not easy for an old man of seventy to be so energetic.

Adhering to the Three Principles of the People: Mr. Fan would translate each paragraph of his speech through a translator. At first, he expressed his views on the Premier's Three Principles of the People, expressing his admiration and adherence, and that it was suitable for modern needs. It is not easy for Mr. Fan to understand the Three Principles of the People so clearly and have a deep understanding of them. The translator's eloquence is excellent. It took several hours, so the listeners were not tired at all.

Excellent Words in the World: He criticized communism a lot, saying that those people only use violence to hold the world, regardless of the situation in various places. For example, a woman is pregnant and should wait for her to mature and give birth, so that her children can be healthy. Now, she does not consider this and forces her to give birth artificially in five or six months. How can the result be perfect? The world has not reached the communist era, and forcibly making it red is like this. For a time, the listeners were in an uproar.

Sudden Questions: After Mr. Fan finished his speech, a man in the crowd stood up and asked three questions, saying that Belgium has not yet abandoned extraterritoriality, the British Labor Party's policy does not conform to the theory of the Second International, and Belgians have set up settlements in China, etc. The audience was stunned by his eloquent words. At that time, the chairman believed that the questions were reasonable, so he asked the translator to ask Mr. Fan. Mr. Fan used his attitude of responding to questions in the parliament in the past to calmly answer. It took almost half a sentence, and the meeting was dismissed in cheers.

Machine Gun Cures Tai

— Good Citizen

Who is Machine Gun? Everyone knows it's the nickname of Mr. Yuan Xiluo Chushu, a native of Baoshan, Suzhou. Mr. Yuan is the third child in his family. His eldest brother, Guanlan, was respected for his virtue and conduct. Recently, he passed away in Shanghai due to a minor illness. The sage has withered, and the whole country mourns him. Mr. Chushu has always been known for his uprightness and outspokenness, which was feared by those in power at the time, hence the nickname "Machine Gun." Those who don't know him are initially intimidated by his name, thinking he is sharp and unapproachable. However, upon meeting him, he is found to be kind and approachable. Mr. Yuan is indeed a man who is internally firm but externally humble. He has been a member of the Kuomintang for a long time and was a member of the Tongmenghui (Revolutionary Alliance) in the past. His arguments moved the world, and he was known as a revolutionary activist. Due to his quiet and retiring nature, he preferred not to engage in political maneuvering, seeking temporary fame. After the revolution, he devoted himself to education, serving as the principal of Nanjing Middle School, Suzhou Middle School, and Tongji University Affiliated Middle School for more than ten years. His students are spread all over Jiangsu and Zhejiang. In the spring of the 18th year, he moved from Qidong to Taicang as an official. His integrity and uprightness brought a new perspective to the people of Taicang. He made a small attempt with great success, and after only fourteen months, he left his post. His achievements were remarkable and praised by the people. Mr. Yuan valued emotions. During his tenure, he often gave extremely poignant speeches at commemorative gatherings, gesticulating passionately. The listeners were moved. He said that the thing he hated most in his life was the spread of opium. On the day he took office, he told people that he would do his best to eradicate opium as long as he was in Taicang. Later, he was ordered to set up an opium suppression bureau, accepting reports and taking swift action, not avoiding suspicion or resentment. Although he was hated by a few local gentry because of this, he did not care. A certain policeman had been dismissed for smoking opium. This policeman, who had previously abused his power, was not only dismissed but also engaged in selling opium at home. The clerks and servants in the government colluded with each other and were arrogant. Mr. Yuan found out about this and took the opportunity to arrest him during an inspection tour. He was eventually brought to justice. As a result, corrupt officials restrained themselves. He also arrested a rogue lawyer named Xu, which pleased the entire county. Initially, a relative of Xu was a prominent local figure and had a past connection with Mr. Yuan. When Xu was arrested, someone asked Mr. Yuan what he would do if the gentry came to plead for leniency. Mr. Yuan said that he would still handle the case according to the law because public and private matters should be kept separate, and a wise gentry would understand this. Even if he came, he would not be able to comply. The gentry heard this and did not say a word. However, Mr. Yuan was eventually blamed by the gentry for this. Mr. Yuan lived frugally while in office, always walking instead of using a car. He especially valued agriculture. Whenever there were locust plagues or insect pests, he would personally go to the countryside to inspect the fields and instruct the villagers on how to prevent and catch them. He spoke to them like a father to his sons. He also frequently gathered the villagers to give simple and sincere speeches. Everyone was surprised that they had never seen such an official in their decades of life. His actions were like this. He was fond of leisure and enjoyed flowers and trees. The office had a garden that had been abandoned. After Mr. Yuan arrived, he pruned, arranged, and planted the plants, making it orderly and neat. In his spare time, he would chant poems in the garden for enjoyment. He was good at calligraphy, and those who sought his work came one after another, and he never refused. Later, due to financial constraints and various restrictions, he repeatedly visited his superiors to present plans and strategies, hoping to make some progress. However, his proposals were not adopted. Mr. Yuan did not want to be a useless official, so he resolutely resigned and returned home. He expressed his aspirations in a poem: "Ashamed of having achieved nothing in my year of office, I am troubled by seeking pasture for the people. Everyone laughs at my simplicity in upholding integrity, and can the defense against enemies ever be enough? Fortunately, locusts and insects are no longer seen, but I still feel guilty that the bridge and road have not been completed. Today, I resign and return home, but I don't have an old house like Yuanming." This shows Mr. Yuan's character. On the day of his departure, the people lined the road, sighing that he was a virtuous official. (Refusing Rewards)

Various Aspects of Cheng Yanqiu

— Xingqiu

"Wenji Returns to Han" is Cheng Yanqiu's creation. The story is based on the story of Cai Wenji returning to the Han Dynasty. Although the plot is simple, the production scale is very grand. The lyrics of Wenji's songs in the play are elegant and refined, and the costumes are novel, which is a new approach. The scenes of drinking in the palace and worshiping at Zhao Jun's tomb are both gorgeous and elegant. The ceremonial guards during Wenji's return to Han used the old style, purely imitating ancient times. The singing is complex, with both Xipi and Erhuang tunes. In addition to Yuanban, Kuaiban, and Nanbangzi, there are also three major sections of slow Xipi, Zheng Erhuang, and Fan Tiao. The essence of the singing lies in the original tune of the Eighteen Songs of the Tartar Reed Pipe, which is the most commendable. The lyrics contain sentences with seven or eight characters, and each sentence has the word "兮" (xi). When Yao Qing taught Yanqiu, he created the tunes according to the words. The "兮" in each sentence must be sung immediately after the lyrics without waiting for the erhu interlude, which is very different from the usual Erhuang singing method. Zhen Hui's poem, "Qiu Lang's laughter and tears are wonderful for a woman, and ten thousand people are captivated by the red carpet," is not an exaggeration.

The Sino-French University of the World Academy held a meeting at 6 pm on October 2 to welcome Yanqiu and played ancient music to help the atmosphere. Dr. Zheng Yuxiu organized a costume ball to raise funds for the Liaoxi flood disaster, which is scheduled to be held at the Grand Hotel next week. It is said that Yanqiu will be asked to perform more songs and dances. Yanqiu is chivalrous and righteous and is willing to help raise funds for disaster relief, so we must rely on him.

Someone named Tidao presented Yanqiu with a couplet: "Her teeth and tongue emit jade-like and golden sounds, beautiful and charming," and "Her liver and gallbladder shine like frost and moonlight, clear as autumn." The first line praises her art, and the second line praises her character, which is a good match.

Short News: The old actor Li Chunli is a famous Jing (painted-face male) actor in Shanghai, affiliated with the Samsung Stage. He is naturally kind and benevolent. When poor people ask for his help, he always generously gives. Therefore, people in the opera world praise him. Recently, he was saddened by the devastation of the floods in Northeast China and automatically donated 50 yuan. It is commendable that an ordinary actor can be so courageous in doing good. (Chang)

Letter: To the Editor of the Free Talk section of your esteemed newspaper: Yesterday, your Free Talk section published an article by Mr. Yu Yangzhou, recording two strange events related to me. The so-called strange deeds of mine are not factual. It is true that I study Buddhism, but the things like commanding ghosts and gods, and summoning centipedes are close to witchcraft, which is beyond my ability. Moreover, my sister-in-law does not understand incantations at all. It is even more shocking to hear your newspaper say that my sister-in-law can use incantations to treat illnesses for relatives. I urge you to make corrections. Sincerely, Yuan Xilian

The Biography of Mr. Zhao Tieqiao (3)

— Zhao Guangzu

The party members were unsuccessful in eastern and southern Sichuan, so they moved to western Sichuan and launched a large-scale attack on Chengdu. My father went to Longchang again. The Chengdu affair failed again. Two uncles, Lusheng and Xinyou, and Mr. Zhang Zhixiang and six others were imprisoned, known as the Six Gentlemen. Mr. Cheng Defan died while fleeing to Jiading. Those who fled to Yibin and Pingshan also died. Zhao Erfeng, the governor of Qingchuan, ordered the arrest of the remaining party members. My father fled back to Shuren School. The principal asked two students to escort my father east to Zhongzhou. After a year, when the arrest was slightly relaxed, he returned to Shuren School to graduate. He went west to Chengdu to visit the Six Gentlemen, who were imprisoned in the Chengdu Prefecture Prison and the Chengdu Huayang County Prison. My father bribed the prison guards to get in and out, secretly communicating with the Six Gentlemen and the party members. The Guang'an affair failed again. Mr. Jinfan was seriously injured and came [to Chengdu]. The Qing officials closed the city and searched, and he could not get out. My father hid in the Chengdu County Prison and drank with his uncle Xinyou for seven days before leaving. The party members rose and fell repeatedly, and their momentum was not strong. They went to Sichuan together. My father believed that the party members had action but no propaganda, so they were easily defeated. He created the "Entertainment News" to promote the revolution through literature and art. Uncle Lusheng was in charge of writing in prison, and my father was in charge of issuing it outside. As a result, his reputation gradually grew. Qing officials vaguely heard that Hu Yubin, who robbed Jiang'an, was Zhao's alias and published an order to arrest him.

Two years before the founding of the Republic of China, my father went to Beijing to seek the release of the Six Gentlemen. Mr. Wang Jingwei and Mr. Huang Fusheng were imprisoned for plotting to assassinate the Qing Prince Regent. Many party members in Beijing fled into hiding. My father arrived and set up an organization on Yanwang Temple Street, summoning those who had fled into hiding. They left Nanxiawa and met at Taoran Pavilion to secretly plan things. From then on, this became a routine. He and Mr. Tian Ziqin created the "Guoguang News" to criticize the Qing court for its loss of virtue, implicitly leading the revolution in northern China.

To save the Six Gentlemen, my father consulted with Sichuan officials in Beijing, but they refused. He conspired with Ms. Chen Bijun to rob the Ministry of Law prison to rescue Wang Jingwei and Huang Fusheng, but it did not succeed. He once studied ancient Chinese literature with Imperial Censor Zhao Gengyaosheng. Whenever he asked about party affairs, my father would always shed tears. Zhao Gong asked the Qing court to lift the ban on political parties, but all three memorials were rejected. More than 20 days after the Wuchang Uprising, the Qing court lifted the ban on political parties, and Wang Jingwei and Huang Fusheng were released from prison. More than 20 days later, Chengdu was captured, and the Six Gentlemen were released from prison.

Initially, my father secretly went to Wu Luzhen's army, scheduled to seize Shijiazhuang on September 17 to cut off the Qing army's retreat from Wuhan. He and Zhang Shaozeng's army from Luanzhou would attack Beijing together. On the appointed day, my father and Wang Jingwei went to Shijiazhuang together. On the way, they heard that Wu Luzhen had died. They turned to Tianjin and entered Luanzhou to ask Commander Zhang. However, the day before, Zhang's associate commander, Pan Juying, had received orders from the Qing court to take over Zhang's army. My father and Wang Jingwei pretended to be sent by the Qing Consultative Council to advise Zhang not to lightly discuss state affairs and rushed back to Tianjin.

Warmth in the Heart (288)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Green Bamboo Tears, Her Heart Broken; Red Lotus Scent Fades, a Maiden's Soul Departs

The old man from Ningbo's various methods were originally intended to drive away Cuijun. But in this environment, Cuijun only had two paths: death or escape. A famous scholar once said that marrying a concubine who is not content in her place is like capturing a kingfisher and raising it in a cage. But the kingfisher does not submit to the cage. In the end, there are only two options: either lock it to death in the cage or open the cage and let it fly away. Now Cuijun is a kingfisher. If she is not released, she will die in their house, costing them another coffin. So, in the end, Zhang Yiqing saw that she had become a medicine jar. Fortunately, he had other favorites and did not need Cuijun. Keeping her at home would only be a source of annoyance. The old man from Ningbo sometimes quarreled with Zhang Yiqing and used Cuijun as an excuse. If Cuijun took her own life out of anger, it would be another drowning. Moreover, the old man from Ningbo intended to drive her out. Therefore, Zhang Yiqing adopted the "open the cage and release the bird" approach and let Cuijun leave. He still showed some consideration for their past relationship and let her take her clothes and jewelry. He also gave her 300 yuan. This relationship was considered over. This is the beginning and end of Cuijun's return to the world. Zuo Shicheng met Cuijun again and earnestly advised her that wandering in brothels was not a good thing. She should open her eyes and choose a man. He also knew that she had no choice but to return to the world this time. But after this experience, she would gain some knowledge and experience. Cuijun sighed and said, "Call you a good Second Young Master. We girls in the brothel have already been molded into the shape of a concubine. If people want to marry a formal wife, they will never come to our brothel. As for people from the lower class, we won't marry them. Last time, when I married that Mr. Zhang, although I was young and inexperienced, I wasn't reckless. You see, Mr. Zhang had a wife, but she lived in the countryside and didn't come to Shanghai. I asked many of his friends, and they all said the same thing. In Shanghai, many businessmen are like him, especially people from Ningbo and Shaoxing. I didn't expect him to have an old lover who was the wife of a friend. Although it was an affair, she had such power. The worst thing was that I shouldn't have moved into their house. If I had lived outside, I don't think it would have come to this. Secondly, I am too honest by nature and think everyone is a good person. When I first went in, I thought it was normal for men to have two or three wives. Everyone could live together in harmony. She and Mr. Zhang had a long history. I heard that she had helped him financially in the past. Now, if I am a little humble, it doesn't matter. Even if I roll cigarettes for her, it's okay."

Review of Last Week's Treasury Bill Fluctuations

Initially Showing Promise... Then Weakening... Slight Rise at the End of the Week... Fluctuations Reached as High as 25.8 Taels Last week's Treasury bill market continued its upward trend, but fluctuations were uncertain and precarious. The front end was strong, but the back end was weak, with daily fluctuations exceeding ten taels. It once broke through the 570 tael mark, mainly due to repeated declines in overseas silver markets and exchange rates. At the beginning of the week, large traders covered short positions, and on Tuesday (September 30), the price suddenly reached 577.6 taels. However, on Monday (September 29), the initial morning price was only 551.8 taels. Later, rumors spread that the United States was planning to rescue the silver market and that the Bank of England was planning to propose gold coins to prevent banks from falling further. In particular, speculators such as Indian merchant Qiao Rifu and Wu Mou tended to sell, and some short sellers increased their positions, so the market sentiment weakened, and the price fell sharply, plummeting by more than ten taels to just over 60 taels. By the end of the week, the market slightly improved, and the result was 564.4 taels, an increase of 11.5 taels compared to the previous Saturday. The difference between the high and low prices during the week was 25.8 taels, but market sentiment was erratic, with both long and short positions exerting mutual restraint. The recent total amount was approximately 50,000 taels. The British silver bar fell by 0.125, but there was a return of 0.375 during the week. The US bank price also fluctuated by 0.01, a total decrease of 0.005, while the HSBC listed shilling fell by half a pence. The Japanese exchange rate rose by 0.3333. At the initial settlement price, the spot red bar was initially more than 20 taels higher than the forward price, then increased by 15 taels. However, the trend was normal. The following is a summary of the week's events.

Frequent News of Silver Price Support, Finally Continuing the Upward Trend Since the big bar was unchanged on Monday, the silver price continued to fall, and the initial listing of the shilling was unchanged, then reduced by half a file. The internal market tightened, and Chinese merchants generally sold. As for the November treasury bill, the initial price was 552.5 taels, followed by 1.8 taels. Later, large traders such as Xinhong and Luo Mou covered short positions, so the price increased by ten taels, reaching 561.8 taels, and the market closed at 560 taels. The internal market also tightened, and colleagues rushed to close positions. However, the gold market fell to 572 taels. However, the total return for the market was 15.8 taels, and the rise was explosive. October 1 (Wednesday) was a holiday for the Mid-Autumn Festival, and there was no market, but the silver market rebounded, and the bank was still open as usual. The shilling internal and external markets were still stable, and there were slight sales in the gold industry. On Thursday, both the big bar and the foreign exchange market were unchanged, but the bank foreign exchange market tended to be loose. Although there were hedging activities in the gold industry, the bank's intention to sell was still strong. Afterwards, it hovered around 570 taels, and speculators had different opinions on acceptance and delivery. The next day, the big bar rose slightly, and the foreign exchange market also rose by half. The internal market was also loose, but colleagues were still buying, and the gold market trend was weakening and had retreated to within 565 taels. The day saw a return of 11.1 taels, and the result continued to fall by 4.7 taels, a total decrease of about 9 taels over two days, which was due to the news that the UK was proposing to save the silver price spreading in the market, and people were terrified. The big bar and silver market both rose on Saturday, but the United States tended to sell, and people were still in good spirits, so the gold market trend was firm. By the close of the market, it was 564.4 taels, 1.1 taels better than the day before, and the red bar also increased by one tael. Cotton Yarn Last Week's Cotton Yarn Market Without Special Changes

People's Bids (Early week supported by factory insistence, weekend hindered by spot sales of third-grade goods)

The cotton yarn market has seen no significant changes in the past week. However, the overall situation is unfavorable. The state of the world's cotton industry remains weak, and third-grade American cotton yarn continues to trend downward. Therefore, the Chaozhou merchants have a strong desire to dump their holdings and maintain a calm attitude. However, some manufacturers are still tightening their grip, while a major manufacturer, seeing the global situation deteriorating and still holding inventory, remains indifferent. Only a small portion is extremely optimistic. However, due to the overall trend, it is difficult to maintain support alone. British factories are taking the opportunity to release a large batch of 20-count Five Rams cotton yarn, more than 10,000 bales. With this batch of spot goods on the market, sellers are becoming more confident. Based on the overall trend, there is no prospect of aggressive price increases. However, buyers, optimistic about the situation, believe that current demand may pick up. Therefore, they are buying to build up positions. Currently, both buyers and sellers have considerable power, and competition is fierce. Bids on the exchange initially rose due to factory support, but later weakened due to sluggish sales and a sharp drop in third-grade yarn. As a result, the prices for each month were similar to the previous week. Total transactions for the week were 51,350 bales. Various merchant groups bought a total of 6,733 bales of spot yarn. Last Week's Cotton Bidding Market Remained Firm

Raw cotton sales were sluggish due to Indian cotton encroachment... transactions were sparse.

Short harvests in various regions led to weak shipments... bullish sentiment also existed.

Actual cotton sales became increasingly quiet. Chinese and foreign factories have purchased enough Indian cotton to meet their needs for three to four months. In fact, because of the cheap prices, all traders are eagerly seeking a way out, and market prices are extremely accommodating. According to news from Japanese merchants, Indian cotton is being sold abroad at reduced prices due to factory closures and surplus raw materials. Japanese factories are procuring more than Chinese factories, encroaching on the position of domestic cotton. As a result, transactions on the market are sparse, and the amount of bales is also extremely small. The cotton bidding market remained firm because inland merchants, seeing poor harvests in their local areas, were buying more in the exchange. Although the harvest in Hankou was good, some operators were manipulating the market by not selling, resulting in a slight shortage of supply. Therefore, there were occasional bullish views. However, the large quantities of foreign cotton ordered by various factories are all due in November and December. When they arrive in Shanghai in a concentrated manner, there may be a drastic change. Bids on the exchange were slightly up by two qian compared to the previous week, with distant months remaining stable. Total transactions for the week were 126,400 dan. Factories bought 71,230 dan, and trading firms bought 4,900 dan. The source of goods at the docks included 9,700 bales of Yao cotton and 1,270 bales of general cotton. Last Week's American Cotton Remained Uncertain

A New York cable report on the cotton market for the past week stated that the cotton market saw an increase in hedging and liquidation by near-month bulls, causing the market to fall sharply. The October contract nearly fell below 10 cents. However, as the market fell, hedging activities immediately provided support. At the same time, industry buying and short covering also occurred. Furthermore, with the actual situation improving, market prices rebounded by half a cent. However, as prices rose, buyers also exited the market. Therefore, the overall trend remains uncertain. As for group accounts, they believe that agricultural product prices are generally weak and remain indifferent to hoarding. However, the chairman of the Agricultural Adjustment Administration, Mr. Legge, said that in his personal opinion, this is a great opportunity for those who want to stockpile goods. Grain Market: Rice Market in Hexia Turns from Stable to Rising

Packaging for Export Transactions Resumes

Zhabei: Yesterday, there were more than 20 ships from the inland route. Sales on this street were extremely brisk, and there were also businesses packaging and transshipping to Qingdao. Due to the tight supply of production information, cargo owners are more inclined to sell at higher prices. As a result, new japonica rice immediately rose by 2-3 jiao. Special grade goods have already been offered at 17 yuan outside the Customs, with ordinary grades offered at 16.5 yuan. The market situation is quite good. Dongxin goods are very scarce, and large quantities are also in short supply, offered at 15.45 yuan. The price of new Sheep Tip rice has risen sharply, with customer demand, leading to a rise of about 4 jiao, reaching a high of 13.78 yuan. Dujian rice is 14 yuan to 13.8 yuan, also increased. Butip rice is 11.78 yuan, and Ketip rice is 11.5 yuan. All of the above have risen by 2-3 jiao. Because these goods are retailed by shops and restaurants, competition is keen, and transactions are smoother. The bottom stock has slightly decreased. Currently, the japonica and indica markets are about to turn sideways. The price of Baiyuan goods remains at 17.8 yuan. Baige paddy is sold as soon as it arrives. The market is not yet active, with prices around 16 yuan.

South Shanghai: Yesterday, about 30 ships arrived from the river, and sales were still good. The market for new japonica rice has become firmer, with high-grade goods at 16.5 yuan. Sales of ordinary Su-Tong japonica rice were sluggish, and prices increased slightly. The overall trend is similar to the previous session. The quality of japonica rice arrivals is uneven, and buyers' and sellers' perspectives are different, so price fluctuations are frequent. The market situation varies accordingly. Sales of South Shanghai Baige paddy and early rice such as Yishixing are not very smooth, and the situation is barely stable. The amount of high-grade Sheep Tip and Dujian rice arriving is extremely small, with ordinary grades predominating. Demand is not smooth, and the price of extra-high-grade goods is offered at 12 yuan outside the Customs. There is no sign of a change in the stability of Biyuan.

Sugar Market: Japanese Sugar Showing a Downward Trend

Yesterday's sugar market saw no cables from the production area due to the weekend. Market trading was sluggish. There was little interest in No. 24 Dutch sugar, coarse granulated white old goods. Finely ground granulated white sugar was at 8 liang 0.5 fen, and No. 20 medium granulated white sugar was at 7 liang 7 qian 5 fen. Demand was weak, and the market was flat and dull. Japanese sugar imports and exports were also sluggish, and the market showed a gradual decline. Mark prices were at 7 liang 9 qian 5 fen for M mark, 7 liang 8 qian for TK mark, 8 liang 1 qian for Liao mark, 7 liang 8 qian for YT mark, and 7 liang 6 qian 5 fen for TN mark. There were few buyers, sales remained sluggish, and the trend indicated a downward inclination.

Local News

Mr. Fan Diven's Speech Yesterday on World Peace

Only Democracy Can Defeat Autocracy; Then World Peace Can Be Permanently Guaranteed

Yesterday at 4 PM, Mr. Fan Diven, Chairman of the Second International and former Foreign Minister of Belgium, gave a public lecture at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce on North Henan Road, titled "The Question of Peace." Accompanying Mr. Fan were Cai Yuanpei, Wang Jingqi, Wang Xiaolai, Yang Gongda, and the Belgian Minister to China, Hua Luosi. The majority of the audience were students, numbering about several hundred. Excerpts from Mr. Fan's speech are recorded below:

Cai Yuanpei's Introductory Remarks　 Cai Yuanpei first delivered an introductory speech, stating that Mr. Fan Diven was born in 1866 and studied law, political economy, and sociology at the University of Brussels. At the age of 19, he obtained a doctorate in law and worked as a lawyer in Brussels. He joined the Labor Party and soon made it the most powerful socialist party in Belgium. In 1894, he was elected as a member of the House of Representatives and has remained in the parliamentary seat as the leader of the Socialist Party. From 1900 to 1918, he served as a professor at the University of Brussels. From 1916 to 1918, he was the Minister of Food Supply. From 1918 to 1921, he was the Minister of Justice and Vice-Chairman of the State Council. From 1925 to October 1927, he served as the Minister of Foreign Affairs and Vice-Chairman of the State Council. Mr. Fan's theories combine the ideas of Karl Marx and Friedrich Engels from Germany, and Henri de Saint-Simon and Pierre-Joseph Proudhon from France. His economic views aim to abolish the capitalist system and private property, promote trade unions, temporarily allow the existence of small businesses and small landowners as a transition, and ultimately achieve public production and public consumption. His political views advocate universal suffrage as a means to obtain political power and the enactment of social legislation as a precursor to reform. In the International Socialist Congress held in London in 1896 and in Paris in 1900, Mr. Fan was already one of the most important leaders of the party. The issue of how to maintain international peace was of utmost importance at the meeting. After the European War, Mr. Fan especially devoted himself to the restoration of international peace, actively upholding the League of Nations and participating in the International Labor Bureau. His sincerity in loving peace is evident. Today's lecture on the theme of peace must have important implications and enlighten us. Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the Premier of the Chinese Kuomintang, said in his doctrine of nationalism that the inherent morality of China includes a love of peace. Even at his death, he still cried out, "Struggle for peace to save China!" This shows the sincerity of our party's love for peace. Surely, Mr. Fan's words will be in agreement with ours. We now wish to invite Mr. Fan to enlighten us.

The Treaty of Versailles　 Mr. Fan then rose to speak amidst applause, translated by Yang Gongda, stating that he and the Czechoslovak Foreign Minister, Weierfu, had signed two important peace treaties, one being the Treaty of Versailles and the other being the Treaty of Locarno in 1925. The Versailles Peace Conference was convened after the end of the European War to resolve future peace issues. At that time, China and Belgium had special diplomatic interests in the conference due to their contributions to the war, that is, they could speak and make requests within the conference. However, the power of recognition and decision-making remained in the hands of the five powers of Britain, France, the United States, Italy, and Japan, with Britain, France, and the United States having the greatest authority, hence the name "Conference of the Three Heads." After the opening of the conference, the French representative was the most forceful, stating that the conference should be based on the opinions of the victors and that the conditions decided could not be changed after they were proposed. The German representative had no choice but to succumb to the power and painfully accept the conditions. Therefore, the Versailles Peace Conference was not a truly consensual peace, but a forced peace backed by military force. However, five years later, the Locarno Peace Conference was reconvened, and the atmosphere changed. The British representative, Chamberlain, was able to consider the interests of all European countries. The German representative, although extremely forceful, was also very gentle. The French representative, Briand, also advocated humanitarian peace. Therefore, the result of the conference was a consensual and guaranteed peace, not a forced peace, which was absolutely different from the Versailles Peace Conference.

No War Recently　 Since the successive signing of the two treaties, Europe and the whole world have been able to maintain peace to a certain extent. However, local and partial small wars have occurred from time to time, which we cannot deny. Fortunately, none of them have affected the whole world. According to my personal observation, I dare to say that there will be no war in the near future regarding the horror and danger of future wars. I met the President of Czechoslovakia in Geneva and also inquired about this issue. He said that it would never happen because the raw materials for war were used up during the European War. With the source cut off, how could fire be generated? This statement completely coincides with my own opinion. If a country insists on defying the great injustice of the world and provoking a world war, it may be possible in theory, but the country's material economy and the people's psychology will not allow it, and it will inevitably lead to bankruptcy and failure.

Guarantee of Peace　 As for the guarantee of future peace, there must be one condition, that is, whether the forces of peace can overcome the forces of war. Otherwise, war cannot be avoided. In today's world peace plan, one is the Second International, which advocates cooperation among all ethnic groups in the world to overthrow autocracy and aggression to maintain and guarantee future peace. Another is the League of Nations. The League of Nations has indeed done considerable work in banning alcohol and other economic reforms and social undertakings. However, I have deep doubts as to whether it can truly maintain peace. The fact that the two major countries, the United States and Soviet Russia, have not joined the League of Nations is a major shortcoming. The United States of North America, including many ethnic groups, is implicitly another League of Nations. The Soviet Russian Social Federation can become a League of Nations. If China creates a federal China in the future, then China, with its vast land and abundant resources, can also be considered a League of Nations. Recently, Briand proposed a European Federation plan. If it can be realized, it will be another League of Nations. I generally agree with Mr. Briand's plan in principle, because Europe is in an era of group competition. If it is not united in terms of economy and materials, it will inevitably fail and go bankrupt in the future. However, when it will be realized is only a dream.

European Federation Plan　 There is a prerequisite for the realization of the European Federation plan, that is, countries with a common political organization should be united first. However, today's Europe has one type of country that is democratic and another that is autocratic. Can two extremely opposite political organizations be united? Therefore, it is said that realization is equal to a dream. If the European countries can still uphold the League of Nations and unite under the League of Nations, then success may be hoped for.

Permanent Peace　 To know whether peace can be maintained in the future and in the near future, it depends on whether democracy can defeat autocracy in the future. Otherwise, it is either a dream or completely hopeless. I admire China twelve million times. If the whole country can truly uphold the Three Principles of the People and be truly loyal to the Kuomintang, then when that day comes, not only will imperialism be completely overthrown throughout the world, but there will be no oppressed ethnic groups and no oppressor ethnic groups, and world peace will be permanently guaranteed.

Itinerary of the Hangzhou Tour　 After Mr. Fan finished his speech, he attended a tea party hosted by the Belgian Consul. Tonight, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce will hold a banquet for Mr. and Mrs. Fan, and Cai Jiemin, the Belgian Minister, the Belgian Consul, Zhu Shaoping, Yang Gongda, and others will be invited to accompany them. Tomorrow night (the 7th) at 11 o'clock, they will take a special train prepared by the Ministry of Railways to Beijing. Mr. Fan also invited the Belgian Minister and his wife, Counselor Xue, Zhu Shaoping, Xu Kuanfu, Yang Gongda, and others to accompany him. It is also heard that Mr. Fan plans to take a plane back to Shanghai with the Belgian Minister, while Mrs. Fan and the Belgian Minister's wife will return to Shanghai by train. Yesterday, the Hangzhou side specially dispatched Mr. Peng from the Municipal Government to Shanghai to contact Mr. Zhu Shaoping on reception matters. They tentatively plan to go to Hangzhou on the 12th, stay at the Xiling Hotel, and be entertained by the Provincial Government in the evening. On the morning of the 13th, they will give a public lecture, attend a banquet somewhere at noon, and visit the mountains in the afternoon. On the morning of the 14th, they will give a lecture at Zhejiang University, attend a banquet somewhere at noon, and tour the lake in the afternoon. On the same day at 6 o'clock, they will take the night train back to Shanghai. On the 16th, the Pan-Pacific Association will invite Mr. Fan to give a lecture at the Cathay Hotel at noon. The Question of Installing Electric Lights on Zhongshan Road

The Impact of Road Construction Beyond the Boundaries

Since the completion of the construction of Zhongshan Road in western Shanghai, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works has started to install electric lights. From Longhua to Hongqiao Road, it is handled by the Nanshi Electric Light Company. From Hongqiao Road to Suzhou Creek and the areas north of the creek, it is installed by the Zhabei Electric Light Company. The company had previously dispatched workers to install the ground wires. However, the police of the concession, due to the fact that Hongqiao Road and Xilu, etc., were related to road construction beyond the boundaries, dispatched a large number of armed police to stop the project at the intersections of the roads. The police district in charge also dispatched police to guard the area, forming a confrontational situation. Although the authorities repeatedly negotiated with the police of the concession afterward, the matter has not been resolved so far. Therefore, the ground wire project is still shelved. It is now known that all the utility poles along the road have been completely erected, even at the intersections of Hongqiao Road and Daxilu. However, the electric wires and light bulbs have not yet been installed. It is expected that they will be installed soon. In the future, when the electric wires are connected on the road, the electricity of the towns and factories in western Shanghai can be recovered and supplied by the Chinese territory, recovering the electric power rights and interests.

Wang Jingqi Hosted a Banquet for Fan Diven Yesterday

Dr. Wang Jingqi, the Minister to Belgium, hosted a banquet for Mr. and Mrs. Fan Diven, the former Foreign Minister of Belgium, and Mr. Hua Luosi, the Belgian Minister, at the Dahua Hotel yesterday afternoon. The guests included Cai Jiemin, Di Pingzi, Qian Xinzhi, Yu Rizhang, Qi Yunqing, Hu Mengjia, Zhang Zhuping, Liu Zhanen, Wu Shan, Li Baiyu, Lin Yutang, Liu Yunfang, and their wives, totaling over a hundred people. Halfway through the meal, Mr. Wang delivered a speech, saying, "Mr. Fan, Mrs. Fan, during the tense times of the European War more than ten years ago, our friend July Destree worked hard to come to China from Siberia to give lectures on European politics and the reasons for fighting with the Allied Powers. We often saw him. After the war, we discussed how to proceed, academic exchanges between China and Belgium, and how the European People's Party and the Chinese People's Party should assist each other in the struggle to promote the opening of the minds of the people. Therefore, for ten years, the Chinese Embassy in Brussels has had the closest relationship with famous professors in Belgium. President Cai has stayed in Belgium for a long time and has also strongly advocated it. I am particularly pleased that Mr. Fan is coming to China to give lectures, because it is in line with our long-held ideal of enabling direct contact between people and direct understanding between people. Now we have used the method of academic cooperation to make a starting point. Mr. Fan should see during this trip to China that China greatly respects Belgium, first because Belgium has provided much assistance to China's new construction in the past, and second because hundreds of Chinese children have studied in Belgium. The Alumni Association expressed that kind of personal admiration the other day, which shows that they deeply worship and are very grateful to the place where they originally studied and the teachers they listened to as children. Mr. Fan can also see that China in the past liked to study new knowledge and compare theories. The Kuomintang of Belgium, like Mr. Fan, has been fighting for the oppressed throughout his life, and naturally understands the current situation in China. Personally, I hope that Mr. Fan will bring back a feeling when he returns to Europe, saying that although China is still in a difficult transition period, it will soon be on track and start the Three People's construction, and soon have a peaceful and prosperous China that can work together internationally for many peace works. I now, in addition to celebrating the health of Mr. and Mrs. Fan, also hope that the cultural contact between China and Belgium will become closer and closer, so that all workers in the East and the West, whether they are mental or physical, regardless of class, can work together to create an enlarged nation of universal harmony." Then Mr. Fan answered the speech, which was translated into Chinese by Mr. Yang Gongda. They took photos and dispersed happily at 3 o'clock.

A Brief Account of Mr. Subereff's World Tour

Two Years of Travel, Tasting Hardships

Soon Returning to Announce Success

The Mainland Daily reported that Mr. Subereff, a Westerner, set off from the front of the YMCA in this city on November 7, 1928, alone on a motorcycle, suffering from hunger, thirst, bandits, and other difficulties, touring the world for nearly two years. He has now arrived in Vancouver, Canada, and will soon cross the ocean and return to Shanghai to announce his success. When Mr. Subereff departed, he only carried twenty yuan with him and had no other belongings. After passing through China and entering the territory of Siam, he passed through a swampy, miasmic, and ferocious beastly land that no white man had ever passed through, lasting twenty-four days in total, which was the most dangerous part of the journey. When he arrived in the Straits Settlements, the road was smooth. From Penang to Singapore, he averaged 124 miles per day, setting a new record for motorcycles. When he arrived in Singapore, the local officials personally came out to welcome him, and the local people warmly received him. Therefore, his old car was worn out, so he bought a new car. A German named Boros was willing to drive with him, so they set off together. However, only a hundred miles away from Singapore, the German injured his leg when his car overturned and stayed in the hospital for treatment. Mr. Subereff continued his journey alone, passing through Yangon, Calcutta, Mumbai, and Lahore, and arrived in Karachi. He traversed 787 kilometers of desert land between Lahore and Karachi by motorcycle, which had never been done before. When he arrived in Karachi, the welcome was more grand than in Singapore. At one banquet, a British official specially presented him with a new car, which is the one he is currently riding. Afterwards, he encountered the plight of the Gu'er tribe and other bandits in Persia. Fortunately, the car was fast enough to escape danger. When he arrived in Baghdad, he crossed 900 kilometers of the Arabian Desert to Dama Village. From there, he passed through Syria, Palestine, France, Italy, Yugoslavia, Hungary, Czechoslovakia, Germany, Belgium, England, America, Canada, and other countries. He has now arrived in Vancouver and will set off for Shanghai in a few weeks, returning to his destination to announce his success.

Shanghai County Inland River Ship Registration Regulations

The Shanghai County Construction Bureau formulated the Shanghai County Inland River Ship Registration Regulations, which will be implemented this month, starting registration from the 1st, and ordered all ship bureaus to come to the bureau for registration within a time limit of one month. If they fail to comply after the deadline, they will be ordered to stop sailing and will not be tolerated. Yesterday, Director Wu reported the start date of registration to the county government for record. The provisional regulations for registration are copied as follows: (Article 1) These regulations are specially formulated for the purpose of developing transportation and protecting navigation ships in this county, and should be followed. (Article 2) All inland river ship companies in this county that operate ships within the territory, whether existing or newly established, must apply to the Construction Bureau for registration and obtain a registration certificate. When applying for registration, they should also submit the following items: (1) Company name; (2) Company location; (3) Name, origin, occupation, and address of the manager; (4) Total amount of capital stock; (5) Ship name and tonnage; (6) Ship length, width, and draft dimensions; (7) Machine horsepower and sailing speed; (8) Route map; (9) Wharf start and end points and passing points; (10) Ship purchase or lease and its value; (11) Ship construction date, shipyard name and location; (12) Registration year and month and Ministry of Communications license number; (13) Name of the ship manager After registration, the bureau will send personnel to investigate the items listed in the application form to verify the facts and submit them to the county government for approval. The Construction Bureau will issue a registration certificate for record. (Article 4) The registration fee for each ship will be temporarily waived. (Article 5) All ships that have already been sailing should apply for registration within one month after the promulgation of these regulations. Those who do not apply after the deadline will not be allowed to sail. (Article 6) If a ship company adds a new ship, it must first apply for registration and obtain a registration certificate before it is allowed to sail. If the company's internal reorganization or transfer of property rights is required, it must be registered separately, and the certificate must be submitted and canceled when it ceases operation. (Article 7) Those who violate the provisions of these regulations will be prohibited from sailing or ordered to suspend business by the Construction Bureau to the county government. (Article 8) These regulations will be implemented after being approved by the county political conference.

Dispute Over Housing in Fuxing Lane

The sixty-plus houses in Fuxing Lane on Mackenzie Road were originally the estate of the Zhao family from Ningbo. Last winter, due to a property division among the Zhao brothers, Mr. Fu, a manager of a certain firm, was entrusted to sell them. Fu, seeing the daily increase in land prices in the area, and knowing that someone had offered 500,000 taels, believed it was a profitable opportunity. He purchased the properties from the Zhao family for 340,000 taels and then resold them to Wing On Real Estate Company for 580,000 taels in July this year. With this transaction, Fu made a profit of over 200,000 taels. However, after purchasing the properties at a high price, Wing On Real Estate Company intends to rebuild them for substantial profit. At the end of August, they issued a notice ordering tenants to pay their September rent and vacate the premises by the end of September. The Tenants' Association of Fuxing Lane, feeling pressured by the company, held a meeting and unanimously demanded that the company postpone the relocation until April of next year. The company refused their request, leading to a dispute. It is reported that both parties have hired lawyers to negotiate, and the outcome remains uncertain.

Continued Report on the Pushen Mountain Villa's Jiangzhe Burial Department

Mr. Wang Junsheng, the director of Pushen Mountain Villa, since being entrusted by Mr. Wang Yiting, chairman of the Shanghai Charitable Organizations United Association in the year of Wuchen (1928), to handle the temporary burial matters at the Jiangzhe border area, has found over 160,000 sets of exposed skeletal remains. For the past three years, burials have been conducted in both spring and winter, and so far, five burials have been completed, burying a total of 29,713 sets of remains. Due to the lack of large sums of money, they have only been able to continuously raise donations and conduct burials in stages. As the winter season approaches, Mr. Wang recently went to Jiaxing Wangjiangjing Puyuan to discuss continued burial procedures this winter with local charitable organizations and gentry, and has obtained concrete plans. However, it has been found that there are still over 100,000 sets of unburied skeletal remains in various places, requiring significant funding. A large sum of money must be raised to bury all of the over 100,000 sets of remains. It has been negotiated with Mr. Wang Yiting to draw a vertical scroll of "Ten Thousand Families and Living Buddhas" and Yi Junzhai to write a couplet with seal script, which have been given to the stone printing shop for brocade mounting as gifts for those who donate to the Jiangzhe burial funds. The Leshan Society has agreed to help raise funds by performing operas. At that time, guests who appreciate the performances will be given a full set of vertical scrolls and couplets, as well as funds for enjoying the moment, to collect fees for burying the exposed remains, so that the skeletal remains all over the place can be buried for peace. Helping charity and appreciating calligraphy are truly two birds with one stone.

Inspection Rules for Electricity Theft Remain Unchanged

The Huashang Electric Company, believing that there should be amendments to the rules for inspecting electricity theft and recovering electricity fees from users, submitted a request to the Construction Committee. Yesterday, the company received instructions from the Construction Committee, stating that amending the rules was not approved and providing a detailed rejection of each clause. The rejected clauses are excerpted as follows: (1) Criminal law has specific provisions for electricity theft. When a company discovers electricity theft, it must submit the case to the court for investigation, which is a legal procedure that cannot be violated. As for the company's recovery of electricity fees, according to the provisions of Rules 5 and 6, it can be directly recovered, forming an incidental civil lawsuit. However, the criminal part still needs to be judged by the court to comply with the principle that guilt must be punished. It is not appropriate to disregard national laws due to the company's cumbersome procedures. Regarding whether the judge's punishment is appropriate, that is another matter. (2) The calculation method for recovering electricity fees is very clear in the various articles of the rules. If there are concerns that the judge lacks electrical knowledge, electricians can be invited to provide expert opinions as evidence. (3) Calculating electric lights for 12 hours and electric fans and heaters for 6 months is a general provision. If it can be proven that there are special circumstances in the city, such as using electricity for more than 12 hours or 6 months, it can be calculated according to 24 hours a day for the whole year. Even if non-users steal electricity without meters, it can be calculated according to wattage and horsepower. The rules already have clear regulations. (4) Although the company has many users, if inspections are conducted effectively, it should be possible to detect all cases of electricity theft. It is extremely rare for users to steal electricity completely after meter installation, causing the meter to not move at all. If it is not because the company's meter is inaccurate and there is indeed electricity theft, it can be handled according to Article 5 for non-user electricity theft. When users apply for transfer of ownership, the company should send personnel to verify the authenticity. How can it be allowed to be obscured? (5) The rules stipulate the act of electricity theft and the calculation method for recovering electricity fees. Whether to stop supplying electricity after discovering electricity theft should be stipulated in the regulations for cracking down on electricity theft. Before these regulations are announced, the original procedures can be temporarily followed.

Party Department Seals Must Follow Regulations

The Shanghai County Party Department received a notice from the Provincial Organization Department yesterday, stating that the department has previously issued a notice regarding the seals of various departments and offices of county party departments in accordance with central regulations. Recently, it has been found that many counties have not complied with the regulations, and the size and style of the seals are inconsistent, which is inappropriate. A notice is hereby issued again to ensure compliance in the future. The details are as follows: (1) The seal should be made of wood and square, measuring 1.6 inches; (2) The size should be measured according to the construction ruler; (3) The width of the seal border should be one-tenth of the size; (4) The seal text should be in Yang Seal script; (5) The text should read "Executive Committee/Party Affairs Reorganization Committee of the [Province] [County] Branch of the Chinese Nationalist Party [Department Name] Seal." Those whose style is non-compliant should immediately re-engrave and submit for verification to demonstrate caution. When directly issuing documents or submitting forms, the department seal should be properly affixed to ensure accountability. Please be informed.

Local News II

Shaji Foreign Firm Accountant Embezzles Large Sum and Flees to Shanghai

Embezzling 33,000 Yuan of Public Funds

Bai Rixuan and He Rong are Arrested

Transferred to Guangzhou Court for Trial

Chen Jianji and Bai Rixuan from Guangdong were previously the chief and assistant accountants at the Lide Foreign Firm in Shaji, Guangdong. Recently, they colluded to embezzle 33,000 yuan of public funds and fled to Shanghai. The foreign firm learned of this and sent a letter to the German Consulate in Shanghai, along with photos of Chen and Bai, requesting assistance in their arrest. The German Consulate transferred the photos to the General Inspection Office of the General Patrol House, ordering them to investigate. Chief Ayers instructed Chinese detectives Feng Zhiming, Pang Ruiqing, Wang Chengying, Feng Shuofu, and Zhang Shaoqing to investigate whether any new arrivals from Guangdong were staying at major hotels. The detectives, upon receiving the order, began investigating and finally found Bai Rixuan staying in room 320 on the third floor of the Dongya Hotel on Nanjing Road at 11 PM on the 3rd. The registered place of origin was Guangdong, and it was learned that he was a new arrival. The detectives knew that the Bai person was undoubtedly Bai Rixuan and went to the room to investigate. They saw two people in the room, one of whom was identical to Bai Rixuan. When asked his name, he admitted to being Bai Rixuan. The other person, named He Rong, was a clerk from Lide Foreign Firm and came with Bai this time. The detectives, suspecting him as well, arrested and detained both of them at the patrol house. The next morning, they were escorted to the Criminal Division of the Special District Court. Patrol House lawyer Ru Baoyi explained the case, stating that the incident occurred in Shaji, Guangdong, and all the evidence was there. If the case was handled by the court, the investigation of various evidence would be quite complicated. It would be better to transfer the case to the Guangdong court for handling, but the patrol house also has difficulties in the transfer. Therefore, the patrol house thought of a way: the patrol house notified the Municipal Public Security Bureau, ordering them to send detectives to the case, take the two criminals away, and transfer them to Guangdong. The procedures seemed more convenient. Today, Director Yuan of the Municipal Public Security Bureau has officially sent detectives to the case, and it is expected that the presiding judge will also agree, etc. Therefore, the detectives reported the circumstances of the arrest, and the detectives from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Wang Shenqing, delivered the official documents requesting the transfer. When questioned, the defendants denied embezzling public funds. Judge Xu Jiashi verified the confession and ordered Bai Rixuan and He Rong to be handed over to the detectives to be taken back and transferred to the Guangzhou court for trial.

Judgment in Tang Huixuan's Lawsuit Against His Wife for Adultery

Tang Huixuan, a Ph.D. in economics, filed a lawsuit in the Criminal Division of the District Court against his wife, Zou Aizhen, and Chen Genwei for adultery. The trial was conducted publicly by Judge Wu Zhen. As a result, the court ruled that the suspicions alleged by Tang could not be proven, and Zou and Chen were found not guilty. The original text of the judgment has been obtained and is transcribed below. Plaintiff Tang Huixuan, 36 years old, from Guangxi, residing at No. 19, Lane 3, Jinchengli, Daxing Street, outside Xiaoximen. Defendant Zou Aizhen, 25 years old, from Shanghai, residing at No. 821, Zhonghua Road. Defendant Chen Genwei, 28 years old, businessman from Shanghai, residing at No. 821, Zhonghua Road. The above-mentioned defendants are accused of interfering with marriage. After the plaintiff filed the lawsuit, this court made the following judgment after trial: (Judgment) Zou Aizhen and Chen Genwei are both not guilty. (Reason) According to the plaintiff Tang Huixuan's testimony, he heard rumors from friends that his wife, Zou Aizhen, and Chen Genwei were having an affair. On August 16th, at 5:00 AM, he brought the police and three others to Zou's house. He went upstairs first and saw Zou Aizhen and Chen Genwei in bed together. He immediately called the police upstairs and arrested Zou and Chen. The defendant Zou Aizhen testified that she lived in the front building with her mother, etc., and Chen Genwei lived in the back building. They first dragged my sister away. I heard the noise and came out, and then they dragged me away. The testimonies of the defendant Chen Genwei and Zou Aizhen's mother, Zou Yu, and sister, Yuezhen, were also the same. The testimonies of the two parties differed. This court summoned the police officer He Fenglin, who accompanied Tang Huixuan to Zou's house at the time. He Fenglin testified that Tang Huixuan ordered him to go upstairs. He went to the entrance of the stairs, and Tang and the people he invited twisted Chen Genwei and Zou Aizhen and handed them over to him to take to the station, etc. Based on this, Zou and Chen were not caught by the police on the spot, but were twisted and handed over by Tang Huixuan and the people he invited. Whether Zou and Chen were twisted in the same bed or in the front and back buildings, the police did not see it in person. The people invited by Tang Huixuan to catch the adultery testified that one was a driver, one was surnamed Xu, and one did not know his name. They did not know their addresses. When asked who the Xu person was, he sometimes said he was his friend, sometimes said he was a friend of a friend, and could not give a concrete name of the friend. His testimony was evasive and clearly untruthful. Based on the above conclusion, the criminal suspicion of the defendants Zou Aizhen and Chen Genwei cannot be proven. According to Article 316 of the Criminal Procedure Law, they should be found not guilty, as in the judgment. This case may be appealed to the Criminal Division of the Court of Appeal. The appeal period is 10 days from the date of service of the judgment.

Rebuilding of the Stone Bridge at the South Gate of Baoshan Completed

Last month, the arsenal sent personnel to use trucks to transport newly manufactured heavy artillery to the seawall outside the North Gate of Baoshan for trial firing. When the truck passed over the stone drawbridge outside the South Gate of Baoshan, the stone bridge was crushed and collapsed into the river because it had been built for many years and could not bear the heavy load. The bridge was about ten feet long and wide, and it was an important thoroughfare from the artillery platform to the city. Since the collapse, pedestrians and vehicles have found it inconvenient. Afterwards, the Baoshan County Government sent a letter to the arsenal to negotiate, and the Baoshan County Construction Bureau designed and surveyed the drawings. The arsenal funded the reconstruction, which was completed yesterday. The bridge piers on both sides are made of stone, and the bridge body is made of railway sleepers. The bridge deck is also wider than the old bridge, and the project is quite solid.

Mid-Autumn Moon Eclipse

Mid-Autumn Festival is on the 8th, not the 6th

There will be a lunar eclipse on the morning of the 8th

Recently, it has been said in the city that the Mid-Autumn Festival is on the 6th of this month, which is purely a fallacy of following the 15th day of the eighth month of the abolished lunar calendar. According to the central government's circular, the Mid-Autumn Festival is the full moon day closest to the autumn equinox, which is the 8th of this month. The old custom of celebrating the Mid-Autumn Festival by enjoying the moon and entertainment is also based on the fact that the autumn season is clear and cloudless, and the moon on the full moon day is particularly round and bright. Therefore, people celebrate the reunion by feasting and enjoying the moon. The 6th of this month is not the full moon day, so where does the reunion come from? It should follow the central government's regulations and take the 8th as the Mid-Autumn Festival, and should not repeat the error of the abolished lunar calendar and enjoy this incomplete moon. It has also been found that there will be a lunar eclipse on the morning of the 8th, which will begin at 0:42 AM on the 7th, with the initial eclipse at 2:46:2 AM, the greatest eclipse at 3:06:5 AM, and the full recovery at 5:31:9 AM.

Wu Yugong, Chen Xingwu, Wang Longchao, and others led them to the manufacturing factory, where chemist Shen Jichuan and pharmacist Zhou Mengbai explained the structure of the machines, the principles of drug manufacturing, the method of extracting and rolling jugal, and the procedures for making Bulida to the visiting guests. The audience was knowledgeable in medicine and pharmaceuticals, so after the visit, they were quite clear and praised the company's complete mechanical equipment and the progress of the pharmaceutical industry, which can be compared with major European and American pharmaceutical factories. Zhao Yichun's family, the owner of the Cui family's Banxianglu at No. 1681 Xinzha Road, was robbed by eight robbers at 6:00 AM on June 12th this year. The robbers stole valuables worth 12,000 yuan. On the 1st of this month, the Old Gate Patrol House's Chinese detectives Huang Fuson and Zhu Ziqing arrested two leaders of the case, Yu Guimao (nicknamed "Little Wuxi") and Zhu Heao (nicknamed "Little Quan'gen"), at the intersection of Dagu Road and Xizang Road, seizing two pistols and ten bullets. Later, the robbers brought the pearls to Zhang's store and sold them for 695 yuan. The patrol house believed that Zhang must have known that the pearls were illegally obtained. How did Zhang know that someone was selling pearls in the Continental Hotel and went to buy them, and whether the robbers had such valuable items? Therefore, he is suspected of receiving stolen goods. Then, the criminals testified that Zhang Fufu was indeed involved in the robbery case, and Zhang Zimei was the one we called to the Continental Hotel. At that time, we falsely claimed that the items were entrusted by relatives in the countryside for sale, etc. Judge Zhou Han verified the report, questioned the two defendants, and ordered the case to be adjourned for trial. twenty-one years old. She came to the Zhu family as a child bride at the age of nine, and the marriage was consummated at sixteen. and falsely accused their daughter-in-law of not being affectionate towards her husband, leading to discord. Man Floating in the River

Soldier Rescued from Murderous Attack in the River

Escapes Death and Rejoices in New Life

Yang Zongjiong, the Commissioner of the Jianghai Customs Tongru Sub-Bureau, came to Shanghai from Nantong a few days ago aboard the Dada Company's Dade steamer. When the ship reached the mouth of the Yangtze River, Yang was taking a stroll on the ship when he suddenly saw a man floating in the river. He immediately instructed the ship's crew and others to pull the man out of the water. Upon examination, it was found that he was a soldier, and his hands and feet were bound. He was barely breathing and on the verge of death. Yang immediately performed emergency surgery to remove the water from his stomach, allowing him to regain consciousness and escape death. After the ship arrived in Shanghai, Yang instructed Fu Yu, a member of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team, to take the man back to the team. During preliminary questioning by Chief Xu, the man identified himself as Qu Bing, twenty-six years old, from Guangxi. He stated that he was a soldier in the 61st Division of the National Revolutionary Army. A few days ago, he had boarded the Xinli steamer from Guangdong to go somewhere on official business. During the journey, he had a dispute with a colleague, who then had him bound, stole thirty yuan, and threw him into the river. Fortunately, Commissioner Yang saw him and rescued him, otherwise he would have drowned. The captain, recognizing that this involved an attack on a traveler, immediately prepared a document to be submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting that arrangements be made for the man's safety.

Prosecution of Counterfeit Wine Sales

The French company Longdong, represented by lawyer Plumey, filed a lawsuit in the French Court stating that they had recently discovered that a Westerner named Tu Mengchuan, residing within the jurisdiction, was counterfeiting wine produced by the plaintiff's company and colluding with Win Si Deng to sell it. Therefore, they reported this to the police station, who searched the homes of the two defendants and seized three hundred and forty bottles of counterfeit wine. The counterfeit wine is now presented as evidence, and it is requested that the defendants be investigated for violating Article 39 of the Trademark Law and Article 269 of the Criminal Law, and that the private lawsuit portion of the damages, three thousand yuan, be recovered. The defendant, represented by lawyer Tibek, argued that the wine was actually purchased by the defendant Tu Mengchuan from a German named Jia in Tianjin from a consignment store and resold to the defendant. An invoice can be presented as proof. Therefore, Tu Mengchuan transported it to Shanghai and entrusted the second defendant to sell it on his behalf, not knowing that it was counterfeit. The damages sought by the plaintiff are excessive, and the defendants were not aware of the situation and were not the counterfeiters. Therefore, they should not be punished. A fair investigation is requested. Chinese and Western officials ordered them to leave and await sentencing.
