Payday Robbery Narrowly Averted at Arsenal

The Shanghai Arsenal workers' wages, originally scheduled to be issued on the 5th of each month, were issued earlier for the month of September due to the Mid-Autumn Festival and yesterday being Sunday. Director Guo, out of consideration for the workers, arranged for the wages to be distributed on the 4th. The wages for the workers of the Longhua Arsenal branch, totaling over 25,000 yuan, were entrusted to the payroll committee member, accountant, and factory guard Xu Xibao, who carried the money in a self-owned No. 3 car to the Longhua factory. Unexpectedly, as the car passed a small wooden bridge opposite the Southwestern Yang Middle School on Longhua Road, another car carrying six or seven robbers suddenly drove towards them. One robber fired a gun and shouted for them to stop. The Arsenal car member and the guard Xu Xibao realized the situation was bad. Xu Xibao pulled out his pistol and returned fire, while instructing the driver to drive at full speed. After exchanging fire for about a minute, one robber was shot and fell inside the other car. The factory guard Xu Xibao sustained two bullet wounds to his right leg, but was not seriously injured. The robbers saw that the car was speeding away and difficult to approach, so they fled. The factory car drove straight to the Longhua factory, and the wages were not lost. The wounded factory guard Xu Xibao was sent to the Arsenal's military medical department for treatment. Director Guo was notified, and fearing there was an inside connection, he has sent men to conduct a thorough investigation.

Investigation of Soybean Cake Sales in Shanghai by Eastern Provinces

Seeking to promote domestic sales, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce received a letter yesterday from the Economic Investigation Bureau of the Harbin Chinese Eastern Railway, stating, "The daily necessities of the people in the Eastern Provinces rely heavily on foreign goods. This is a great problem. Fortunately, the region produces abundant soybeans, soybean oil, and soybean cake, with an annual export of 4.12 million tons to foreign countries, providing a much-needed source of revenue. In recent years, immigrants from within the country have arrived in large numbers, reclaiming barren land and increasing production. However, the foreign sales routes for soybeans, soybean oil, and soybean cake have suddenly become sluggish. At the same time, according to customs trade records, the amount of soybeans, soybean oil, and soybean cake imported into domestic ports from foreign countries is very large, while domestic exports are declining. The current situation is precarious. Thinking about the future, we are very worried. Our bureau, concerned about the difficulties of the times, has conducted extensive research and believes that it is necessary to adhere to the principle of agricultural division of labor, and to promote the domestic sales of soybeans, soybean oil, and soybean cake from the Eastern Provinces through transportation policies. At the same time, the Eastern Provinces can exchange domestic products for their daily necessities, so that both benefit and the outflow of revenue can be stopped. However, this matter is of great importance and has many complexities. Without knowing the truth, problems are inevitable. We should send personnel to conduct on-site investigations in the future so that they can be accurate and feasible. As we set out, we have long admired your chamber's concern for the country and its attention to economic matters, and we specifically list the following points to request your busy schedule for review, so as to provide a basis for progress. If it can be realized in the future, the country's economy and people's livelihood will truly benefit." Attached are the investigation points: (1) Does your port produce soybeans, soybean oil, and soybean cake? What is the production volume? Where is it sold? If there is no production, where does it come from? (2) What is the selling price per catty, per shi (please specify the weight of the shi), or per dan in silver dollars? What are the tax rates? What are the major fluctuations each year, and what are the reasons for the fluctuations? (3) What technology is used to convert soybeans into soybean oil and soybean cake (traditional methods or machinery)? What is the current manufacturing capacity of the city? (4) What are the common uses of soybeans, soybean oil, and soybean cake, and are there any new uses being invented? (5) Do farmers view planting as a main occupation or a secondary occupation? (6) What is the transaction method, and are there any groups or large-scale trading firms? (7) Are there any soybeans, soybean oil, or soybean cake from the Northeast that flow into the market? If so, what are people's comments on them? Is there a possibility of expanding in reality? If there are direct sales, can the capital be compatible? What are the transportation costs? (8) What products does your port sell to the Eastern Provinces? Are there any obstacles to sales? (9) What are the great opinions of your council on this matter? We have heard that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has already forwarded the letter to the Soybean and Grain Merchants Association for detailed investigation and reply.

Request to Deduct Shanghai-Taiwan Relief Funds

In the past year, Zhejiang Province held a relief donation campaign, ordering all merchant ships traveling in Zhejiang to collect a 10% relief donation on passenger fares. The Shanghai-Ningbo, Shanghai-Wenzhou, Shanghai-Taiwan, and inland river small steamers traveling to various ports in Zhejiang sent letters to the Navigation Association, explaining the difficulties of each line and submitting them to the provincial government. Representatives were also sent to Hangzhou to petition separately. Subsequently, the Zhejiang Provincial Civil and Construction Departments drafted measures, and the provincial government decided to consider the difficulties of each line and approved separate handling. The Shanghai-Taiwan line merchant ships carrying relief donations were allowed to deduct and return 10,000 yuan of donations already donated by the companies to the Taiwan Disaster Relief Association. The Navigation Association forwarded the letters to each shipping line and company to comply. Previously, the relief donations carried by the Shanghai-Taiwan line had exceeded 10,000 yuan. Therefore, a list of seven points requiring inquiry regarding the deduction of donations was presented to the Zhejiang Provincial Government by the Navigation Association on September 2nd for approval. Since the approval had not been received for a long time, a document was prepared yesterday to urge them. The bottom of the presentation is as follows: The presentation is for the purpose of urging and requesting a prompt review and approval of the measures for deducting the carried relief donations, so that they can be followed. The association previously presented a report on September 2 regarding the Shanghai-Taiwan shipping line merchant ships carrying relief donations, approved to deduct 10,000 yuan of donations already donated to the Taiwan Disaster Relief Association, because the donation situation of each merchant ship is different, and where the remaining donations after deduction should be handed over, which is related to the relief donations, so we have to be extra cautious. However, to this day we have not received a review and approval, so we continue to present this matter, humbly requesting you to inspect and approve it promptly so that we can comply and are extremely eager. Respectfully presented to the Zhejiang Provincial Government.

Investigation of Silk Factories Closing

Sixty-Five Out of Ninety-Seven Factories Have Closed

Over Thirty Thousand Male and Female Workers Are Unemployed

There are a total of 106 silk factories in Shanghai. Recently, the price of silk per dan has plummeted from over 1,000 taels to around 800 taels, greatly affecting all silk factories. Coupled with foreign competition, the sales of domestic silk have become sluggish, making it increasingly difficult for silk factories to maintain operations. As a result, more than half of them have been forced to close down one after another. According to a survey conducted by the Daily News, out of the 106 silk factories in Shanghai, 97 were surveyed. Among these 97, 65 have already closed. There are over 28,000 unemployed female workers and over 2,500 unemployed male workers. In total, over 30,000 male and female workers have lost their jobs due to silk factory closures. The remaining 35 factories that have not yet closed are also struggling. Approval for Tax Exemption on Products of Electrical and Silk Weaving Factories

The Shanghai Electrical and Silk Weaving Factories Association previously commissioned Accountant Pan Xulun of Lixin Accounting Firm to represent the association's factories and submit a petition to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. The petition requested that various imitation foreign woven products be taxed according to the current regulations for machine-made imitation foreign goods to provide protection. The Ministry has now approved the submission of the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, allowing all of the factory's products, such as Guangya Tili, Ballaige, Xinhua Ge, Xiafei Ge, Xinhua Fang, French Crepe, Boro Crepe, Qi Xiang Crepe, and Xin Ya Jin, to be handled according to the tax regulations for machine-made foreign goods. That is, when these products are sold domestically, they will be subject to the regular export tax and the 2.5% surtax at the first customs checkpoint, after which they will be exempt from further taxes. Exports to foreign countries will be completely exempt from taxes to facilitate sales. This request for tax exemption for silk weaving factory products is unprecedented. However, other factories in the same industry can follow this precedent and submit similar requests.

Lianyi Film

Sickness

— Chun

Sickness is the most detestable thing, yet it has finally assailed me. Of course, I knew that sickness was lurking within a short period, and its signs had already forewarned me, but I only wished to avoid it and not be so entangled. However, the factual arrival of it ultimately violated my ideal, declaring that I am sick.

This is truly unfortunate. My family has all suffered the fate of illness. Even I could not escape. When I made eye contact with the sick, I felt a sharp, stabbing pain. My father is sick, my elder brother is sick, my second elder brother is sick, all groaning in bed, making the harmonious atmosphere of the whole family utterly desolate due to the gloom of sickness. Recently, my mother also fell ill from overwork in caring for them. Logically, I shouldn't have come to this bustling city to toil, turning a blind eye to the sick at home. However, in the end, for the sake of my own future, I had no choice but to leave this home filled with the groans of sickness and rush here and there. Who knew that before Heaven, my lurking illness would also break out, and I would also be groaning in bed?

Naturally, I don't even know what I am busy for, but I believe that there are always some things that are not solely for my own sake. Whenever I meet friends after only a month or so of separation, their first question is always, "Why have you become so thin?" This is partly a well-intentioned consolation, but on the other hand, how much agitation it gives me! Indeed, I simply don't understand why I have become so thin. Alas, so thin...

During this illness, the web of worries naturally bound me. I thought of the sick at home, and my thoughts became more and more troubled, and my spirit became more and more agitated. As a result, the burning fever increased proportionally, and my brain felt as if it were about to explode. The doctor couldn't help but be a little alarmed. Seeing my fever, he thought I might have typhoid fever. In fact, how could I have typhoid fever? Unexpectedly, the school took this as an imperial decree and immediately wrote a letter to my father—my sick father—with deeply hidden insinuations in the letter. How could this not worry my father, thinking that I was really that seriously ill? He asked many people to prepare a way for me to return. On the third night of my illness, two people came one after another. Fortunately, I had recovered slightly by then, or wouldn't it have turned a false alarm into reality? In the end, I sent them away. I believe that on this night, my family members—especially my loving father—must have been extremely uneasy.

The chills and fever have finally subsided. I was then eager to come out again. It turned out that in these few days of illness, I had caused many people to worry, even suspecting something unexpected had happened. When I went to Zhige's residence, he asked in surprise,

"We were just preparing to put an advertisement in the newspaper to find you."

"What? Isn't that too ridiculous?"

"It's been a few days, and we haven't heard from you at all. Everyone has been looking for you, but we can't find you. What have you been doing?"

"Don't you see my face? I'm sick! I could only barely manage to come out today."

After I said this, Zhige seemed to believe me a little, seeming to believe that his previous predictions were wrong.

But my doubts gradually grew stronger. I thought, "Why are they so worried about me?" So I asked Zhige,

"But you thought I was missing?"

"Yes, we thought you might be missing, because hasn't your recent talk been strange? And haven't your recent actions also been abnormal? It's been so many days since we last met, and everyone has been looking for you. Wouldn't that be strange? Today, the more we talked, the more we believed it, thinking that something unexpected had happened to you. If we didn't see you again today, we might really have put an advertisement in the newspaper."

"That would be quite interesting," I said with a cold smile. "No coincidence, no story." Alas, such a thing happened during this illness. It may not be an amusing tale.

Now, in this post-illness period, I know very well that I have not fully recovered my original health. But the driving force of this life does not allow me to enjoy the so-called opportunity for convalescence, and I must toil in this world. My father has sent a letter asking me to go home to recuperate, but in this situation, how can I possibly live a quiet life? Therefore, I have not complied with my father's good intentions. My sisters have repeatedly advised me to take care of my body. After seeing me after this illness, besides saying that I was terribly thin, they didn't seem to be able to say anything else. Wenzhi also earnestly told me to take good care of my body in these few days after the illness and not to run around recklessly anymore. But on the one hand, I gratefully accepted this comfort, and on the other hand, I have communicated their good intentions. In reality, I don't know what to do. As for the so-called source of life, how exactly should I pursue it? This is a difficult problem to solve. I only want to not make my life too empty and to at least complete a part of my life's mission, and this may perhaps be my "struggle for life." In that case, this illness is worth commemorating.

Don't Scold People Without Investigation

— Chen Baoqin

In the September 24th issue of the Japanese publication (Youth Garden), in Lu Xiangxian's article "The Person Living in the Pavilion," the content is nothing more than scolding women for not understanding the true meaning of love and only aiming for money. This is too generalizing. Of course, I wouldn't dare to say that all women don't love money, but we certainly wouldn't admit that all women are money-worshippers, more poisonous than snakes, and causes of ruin. Mr. Lu, if you had added a few quantifying words to the phrases like "women..." in your article, such as "a part," or "according to what I have seen," or even "most," "the majority," then I wouldn't have put down my serious books to babble on so much. But Mr. Lu's words are too generalized, too lacking in investigation, how can I keep silent and allow my fellow women to be slandered?

Now that Mr. Lu has generalized that all women love money, then I want to ask Mr. Lu, "Liang Hong and Meng Guang, raising the tray to eyebrow level" in the Han Dynasty has been passed down as a beautiful tale. Is Meng Guang not a woman? Is Liang Hong not a rich man? Furthermore, Zhuo Wenjun's marriage to Sima Xiangru was willing to sacrifice her original wealth to sell wine by the stove. Is Zhuo Wenjun a man or a woman? To take a more recent example, is Huang Huiru willing to marry Lu Genrong for money? There are countless other women who specialize in focusing on talent, learning, and sincere love, and despise money, I'm afraid you don't know them all. I can very frankly say based on the facts that love is by no means unconditional. The so-called "sincere love is unconditional" is deceitful talk, it is singing a high tune. If you say love is unconditional, why do spouses have to choose, and why is marriage autonomous? Isn't it to suit one's own conditions? Since love is conditional, then, women who have received considerable education, have a noble personality and thought, and have genuine knowledge, their demands on the other party are definitely not money. The main things are of course health, talent, learning, personality, thought, effort, and a spirit of progress. Meng Guang's love for Liang Hong and Zhuo Wenjun's love for Sima Xiangru are an example. Although Liang Hong and Sima Xiangru were a rice pounder and a poor man, they were able to sacrifice everything to love them, so they could respect each other as guests and love each other forever, because the conditions they demanded were permanent. But I absolutely cannot strongly argue that there are no dregs among women. There are indeed many who are among those we despise, such as women with generally unconvinced ideas, often hanging the signboard of female students, beautiful on the outside, rotten on the inside, in their minds, they only know fashion, decoration, extravagance, enjoyment, ease, indulgence, etc., fundamentally they do not know what is called love, so the conditions they demand of the other party, naturally, are nothing more than the various types mentioned above, whoever can supply it will go to love whoever, and men, they also use this weakness of women, so they try their best to obey, fearing they will not be able to reach their goal, to achieve their desires, but once the goal has been achieved, what is desired has been achieved, then they turn their original face, who will pretend again, pretending to be a rich old man, the so-called the wood is already a boat, the rice is already cooked, what methods do you have, to jump out of my fence, unexpectedly, it is not the same as it used to be, the old etiquette has lost considerable authority, there is a group of unfilial people - in the eyes of the believers of the old etiquette - who do not care about the three obediences and four virtues, the concept of chastity, and have to change allegiance to Qin in the morning and Chu in the evening, imitating to buy 　 - to divorce their husbands, this is indeed a clear and obvious fact, it is not allowed to deny, in fact, men's psychology, why don't they know that this kind of women are slaves of money, knowing that they are going to violate it, what must

Page 20

The results of inevitable failure, without adding them to their bodies, who else would they belong to, so, mercantilists, causes of ruin, poisonous snakes, vanity, snobbery, these beautiful names, one after another, are crowned on women's heads, this kind of one-sided harsh blame, is it not too much?

As for you saying that women's hearts are more poisonous than snakes, what is the basis, and how do you see that many men's hearts are not more poisonous than snakes? Women's personality and thoughts, can probably be higher or lower depending on the education and knowledge they have received, but in men, there are many who are good at hiding evil intentions, who are more difficult to observe than women, often very knowledgeable men, his despicable personality, and the means of deception, on the contrary, become more novel and more cruel with the transcendence of learning, try to open the history to see, women have been trampled on by men for thousands of years, it is not a special book, it is really impossible to write out the examples in it, from the monarch, to the people, there is no one who does not use policies to destroy women, or be abandoned because of having no children, or be abandoned because of the decline of color, not only destroy their bodies, but also hurt their hearts, most women are infatuated, once abandoned, they will be humiliated for life, as if they have lost the joy of life forever, this kind of abandonment, applied to innocent women, can be said to be extremely cruel, Shang Lingzi's "Separate Crane Play", Cao Pi and Cao Zhi's "Chu Fu Fu", are nothing more than mourning women who are unjustly 　 abandoned, there are also songs of being abandoned because of the decline of color and love in the poem "Gu Feng", these are all iron evidence of men's abuse of women, it can be seen that there was such a treasure before the Three Kingdoms, down to the Sui and Tang dynasties, this trend is even worse, Emperor Yang of Sui was licentious and immoral, indulging in women, to the extreme, once happy, forever abandoned, Bai Juyi's poem "Shangyang People" is to describe the suffering of palace people, since then, more and more plans have been made to create chastity, foot binding, polygamy, concubinage, no talent is virtue, to oppress women, this is even more unknown how many innocent women have been killed and wronged, plus the original old examples, it is really putting women so tightly bound that they do not dare to move at all, there is also the worry of disaster from the sky, now after our many struggles and struggles, we can only get a little bit of freedom, but at the same time, the trap is also set all over the world, to take recent facts as an example, although Huang Huiru herself has no learning, but she can not value money, break the concept of class to love Lu Genrong, this can also be said to be specializing in love as the goal, but Lu Genrong is ultimately a despicable personality, with deception in his heart, ungrateful, so that Huang Huiru died and was defamed, and was laughed at by the world, and in the past, Ma Zhenhua was not cheated by Wang Shichang, as in the latest case of a bigamy case, it is also the means of cheating to marry B, abandon A, he did not even think that when he pursued A, if A absolutely did not accept his request, how would he feel the pain of unrequited love and curse A, he can not say that he is a person without knowledge, from this it can prove what I said earlier, events like these are recorded in the newspaper in a few days, other events that occur in poor and remote places, and are not recorded, I don't know how many more there are, ah, this is originally the progress of mankind, poisonous snakes and beasts, harming people with ignorance is still the public enemy of mankind, people are the spirit of all things, all have compassion, now for no reason to kill and deceive a part of the same kind of men, is it not more poisonous than poisonous snakes and beasts, moreover, women's abandonment of men, mostly before marriage, men's abandonment of women, mostly after marriage, the loss is which is bigger or smaller, also no need to say, before marriage and abandoned, they will scold her for being more poisonous than a snake, then what should be scolded for being abandoned after marriage, as for those who are abandoned before marriage, can we conclude that the fault lies entirely with the women?

Speaking of the word cause of ruin, which one are you referring to, what disaster have women caused in this era, if you can find many examples in history, but there are also many traitors and thieves among men, compared to them, I am afraid that the disaster caused by men is even more than that of women, how can we say that women are the cause of ruin, in short, in general, there are dregs among both men and women, the bad of women, I have already said it myself, Mr. Lu, don't you think that all of you men are good people, there are certainly not a few who are infatuated, but there are also many people who change allegiance to Qin in the morning and Chu in the evening because of a moment of impulse and temptation, I hope Mr. Lu will think about it next time before scolding (Editor's Note) Mr. Lu's original work is entirely an objective description, not a subjective criticism, Mr. Lu described the wandering life of the bored young people living in the pavilion, humming Beijing tunes, talking about love, shouting poor, ...quite thoroughly, so it was selected and published, now, Ms. Chen has written this article to defend the women's side, this journal will of course also respect it, and publish it as above, to see the general opinion of the women's side on the issue of love,

Overthrow the Idol

— Wen Juan

Because I like to go to the remote places to study the customs of the people, so Yangcheng County, which is far away in the northern border, has my footsteps, this county, only three miles across the city, and there are only three city gates, the north gate is opposite the Daqing Mountain, scholars think that opening the gate will definitely offend the mountain god, so they specially built a high platform on the city wall, called Yangxiang Platform, commonly known as the North Platform, there is a Zhenwu General Temple on the platform, built very carefully, although it cannot be compared with the Da Zhao and Xiao Zhao in Guihua, etc., but it is already much stronger than the houses they live in, in addition to teaching affairs, I often go to the North Platform with my colleagues to change the air, and look at the scenery of the border, the Daqing Mountain is obscured in the north, the Great Wall is like a belt, tied across the waist of the Qing Mountain, there is not a single tree on the mountain, and the rocks are jagged, and the continuous and tall mountain, matched with the yellow sand below for thousands of miles, the howling wind of the Hu wind comes, there is another kind of tragic and magnificent spirit, not something that people who have lived in the south of the Yangtze River for a long time can understand, sometimes when the weather is clear and the sun rises, white clouds are like strands, lingering on the top of the distant peaks, like the Weaver Girl weaving brocade, looking at the slopes everywhere, there are countless white dots vaguely, appearing and disappearing and wriggling there, it is a picture of sheep grazing, sometimes the wind is smooth, you can also hear the flutes of the herdsmen, a Hanhaishi stone is embedded between the turrets on the platform, scholars say, one can see the faces of people a hundred miles away, just go to shine on the people, whoever is thought of in their hearts, can see whoever, but now the spiritual迹 has been pointed out, so it can't be seen, this kind of nonsense is not worth a laugh, but I have to study what is the origin of this kind of fallacy, so I have repeatedly gone to stroke this smooth as glass, brilliant stone, hoping to get some clues, but it is not successful, no reason can be found, later, I suddenly got a little news from many women, because in ancient times, they liked martial arts, Yangcheng was located on the border, and was suitable for the important point of war, the family with strong men often took pride in going out to join the army, so the spring boudoir has dreams, often on the banks of the Wuding River, every thought to find a way to see the face of their husband or children, people who like good things, then create this fallacy to fool women, maybe there are also people who rely on this stone to eat,

Since I have been in this small place, there is really nothing to do, the school building is "leaning in an ancient temple, there are only ten rooms in total, the Buddha statue occupies seven rooms, and the remaining three narrow and bad side rooms are the lecture hall of the women's school, the teacher's office has to entrust the building of the Buddha statue, I am a restless person, I can't help but feel disgusted with these clay sculptures and wood carvings, I often think of ways to remove them, at that time it was the spring of the Republic of China, the customs in the northern border were especially closed, although the provincial authorities said that they wanted to work hard to renovate, but their power was really not as great as the people, the total population of Yangcheng County is less than 100,000, but there are as many as twenty or thirty temples, it seems that all the material resources of the people have been provided to the idols, this is a fact that can never be found within the Great Wall, so I first convinced the county magistrate, and asked him to approve me to overthrow the idols, the county magistrate was a student who had studied abroad, and he was very smooth in doing things, in the end, he agreed to my proposal, and encouraged me to do it quickly, and he himself also promised to help me,

I went back to school and told the students and colleagues about the process, they all clapped their hands and rejoiced, and started to throw away the small mud dolls and beat them, in an instant the eyes were a lot clearer, but what about those big ones, they can't be pushed, they can't be shaken, what to do, we went to recruit workers to fight, but even if we paid a high price, no one came to apply, even the beggars refused, after ten days, we knew that hiring people was hopeless, but I, this stubborn person, would I be willing to give up like this when things have started, no, since the county magistrate has spoken, he should not go back on his word, making me in a dilemma, the result of seeing the county magistrate is that he allocated a batch of prisoners to the school, the wages were paid by the school, four corners a day, more than ten smoke criminals and destitute people were brought to the temple with iron chains, a thin and abnormal tall man opened his mouth first, "Sir, although we are criminals, we still want to cultivate the afterlife, we have suffered in the human world, and we don't want to suffer anymore when we go to the underworld, I won't do things to fight the gods, sir, you listen to them do it," for a time, the prisoners all hung their heads, as if each was calculating their own thoughts, "Don't be afraid, this has nothing to do with you, I called you here, all the misfortunes will be borne by me alone, and it has nothing to do with you," after they heard these very simple words from me, it seemed that they had already reached the heavens, and the worries on their faces were also reduced a lot, but several locals were still making excuses, or using their eyebrows to indicate that they did not want to risk this great danger, I was afraid that they would destroy it again, I looked at the faces of these people in turn, and saw that one of the Shandong people seemed to be more courageous, and also seemed to have a deeper resistance to fate, not believing that not fighting the gods would make his life better, and four corners a day, ten days is four yuan, after all, it is better than sitting in the sky, so he first explained to me that he could do it, but he had to take the money first, I was afraid that he would be slippery, the result of the discussion was that he would pay two corners first, and then take two corners when he left work, so seven or eight unwilling people all went back together, leaving five, and followed me to the East Hall to stand still, this is a place to worship miscellaneous small idols, except for the three sitting, the rest are standing, but only six feet high, in principle, it should not be very difficult to destroy, but the five people took the rope, and they seemed unable to start, I understood, so I walked up and first put the rope ring on the head of the clay man, pulled it hard, and turned back to the crowd and said, "Okay, this has nothing to do with you," they stumbled up and pulled for a long time, a clay man fell down, so they took it out and put it on the barren land in front of the school, half a day's work, only three were gone, and it was only a little more than ten o'clock, they were going to eat, they didn't come until two o'clock in the afternoon, and they all left at four and a half, they did this for several days, the East Hall was finally empty, but those clay corpses piled outside the school also had to hire a car to send them out of the city to be thrown away, the secretary went out to call the car and ran into a lot of nails, saying, "We are afraid of being struck by lightning and dare not pull," I used the old method to persuade them, they also refused, what to do, from the street to the school, a road has been like Shanyin Road for days, crowded with men and women watching the excitement, old women with crutches also came to see, all pointing and surprised at the encounter of the idols they usually worship, and their resentment towards me is as deep as the sea, some people say that I am the reincarnation of the devil, and some people say that it is also the time for the robbery of the gods, recently I was sent by heaven to beat them, the students were banned at home, not allowed to come and get close to me again, fortunately, the provincial government is enforcing compulsory education, the official department can use orders to urge students to go to school, I also asked the county magistrate for help, he had no way, so he had to call people to urge them from door to door, so my good students came together again, later I knew that even if they were not urged, their parents would also send them, because they were all making plans to go on a hunger strike at home, I don't know who taught them, probably their age, has reached the time when they can resist oppression, the high school students in the border, at least sixteen or seventeen years old, after the event, the county magistrate suddenly had a big banquet for his guests, some people found out that the content of his banquet was all to declare that the overthrow of the idol was initiated by the female principal, and had nothing to do with himself, we laughed it off when we heard it, after the teachers and students cooperated and buried the clay men in the open space next to the school, I also fought with them for half a year before leaving this border and returning to the mainland, after thinking about it, I can't help but laugh at my recklessness,

Youth Garden

Farewell

— Mi Luo

——To my colleagues of two years——

Waiting for the bell to ring, only ten minutes remained. The watch in my pocket ticked away, its rhythmic sound clear and distinct. My heart, stirred by it, throbbed wildly, almost in time with the watch's mechanism.

Before me lay an indescribable dreariness. A ray of sunlight, hanging from the corner of the opposite building, seemed particularly weak today, reluctant to leave the corner.

"Tick-tock," the sound continued without pause. My heart, from its feverish throbbing, gradually calmed, then turned numb. But eventually, the sound of the bell startled me awake. I stood up as usual, left my desk, straightened my sleeves, and walked out of the office with a paper package, alongside my colleagues.

"This is the last moment," I thought. "I am about to leave my colleagues of two years." I had already walked out of the door. I wanted to say a few words of farewell to my colleagues, but I couldn't muster the courage. All I could do was nod as I usually did, and勉强say "goodbye."

Remembering the past two years, how could I bear to leave my many dear colleagues? Since I had walked through the bloodstains of life, braving thorny paths and breaking through adverse circumstances to come to Shanghai to study, barely graduating from a middle school, the burden of economic hardship had built up into a towering debt. In reality, it no longer allowed me to study elsewhere. At that time, with the introduction of a cousin, I entered this Shanghai Land Bureau as a trainee. Over the past two years, I have been treated with exceptional favor by the authorities, and have received the support of many, many colleagues, especially Mr. Li, our director, who treated me like a younger brother. He gave me guidance in my studies, encouragement in my work, and led me forward on the path of life with kindness and benevolence. I will never forget him, not even for a moment.

In my work, I have received sincere guidance from many colleagues, so I have not made many mistakes in the past two years, leaving behind a past history. Moreover, I was gradually promoted from trainee to assistant, and then to clerk. My salary also increased from thirty yuan to forty yuan to fifty or sixty yuan. In my impoverished life, this prevented me from experiencing cold and hunger, and the tuition for my evening studies was also obtained from here. Truly, unless I have already lost my conscience, how could I bear to leave this place so easily?

However, I am ultimately leaving this place, betraying earnest and insistent勸挽, and forging ahead regardless of everything. Have I truly lost my conscience? In this place, I have nothing but infinite apologies, and I simply have no words to justify myself.

Thinking that I am already twenty-two years old, I am so alarmed that I cannot have a moment of peace. In my young heart, I couldn't wait to grow up quickly, to be as tall and big as others. But as the years passed, since my father's death, and then my loving mother's passing, my elder sister's illness and death, and my younger brother's death in a hospital, all kinds of adversities came one after another, progressing at the same time as my life history. In ten years of weeping, I have already grown into an adult. Then, my anxiety also grew spontaneously, as if I had an unspeakable shame. I am already twenty-two years old, and people still ask me how old I am, unknowingly. I can only helplessly answer him, secretly blaming him for not being aware, making it difficult for me to answer.

Twenty-two years old has already arrived, and twenty-three years old will come soon. Every day passes in a muddle. What will be the result of my future? The era is in a state of constant flux, as if pushing waves and following the tide, and is in a state of continuous movement that cannot be stopped for a moment. In the blink of an eye, one will fall behind. Moreover, my knowledge is insufficient, and my ability is weak. How can the perfunctory actions of the present be a long-term plan? I am unwilling to admit that I am ultimately an incompetent person. I was originally endowed with a complete body and a little wisdom. How can I let myself down, let down those who expect so much of me? Therefore, the idea of ​​furthering my studies is constantly swirling in my mind. Finally, I resolutely decided that there is simply no other way except "I give up and strive to study."

I resolutely requested to the authorities, firstly, whether I could be allowed to work part-time and study part-time; and secondly, if I could not be allowed, I would resign.

The application was submitted, and the authorities repeatedly advised, saying that part-time work and part-time study were impossible, telling me not to study, and citing many precedents, "Advancement does not necessarily mean further education." I could only thank them for their kindness. In fact, I could no longer have any hesitation. I have to temporarily forget my feelings, betray my kindness, and leave, leave.

The dream of furthering my studies for two years has finally come true today. I only feel my own boldness. Carrying my schoolbag, I walked along Jiangwan Road. The autumn wind has already blown sharply. Touching my pocket, I still have enough to support myself for a few days. "Food, clothing, housing, and transportation are all indispensable," I thought, secretly measuring it.

Indeed, as the authorities instructed, "Education depends on one's circumstances." With my circumstances, the qualifications for further education have long been exhausted. However, I think that not being able to go to school because you don't have money is no different from wasting money when you have it. If I had a wealthy family, lived a life of luxury, and lived the life of a young master, I probably wouldn't have the thought of furthering my studies and making progress. It is precisely because I am poor, that poor children are willing to study. Everything in the world must wait until you have money before you can do it, and it is not necessarily possible to succeed. Only by gradually breaking through thorns can there be a smooth road to walk. I comforted myself in this way when I had no other choice.

From now on, I hereby swear,

"I will forever abandon my sorrow, not worth追維my past. I will turn my thoughts around and no longer sing about snow, moon, wind, and flowers. I will strengthen my consciousness, move forward and follow the banner of the Chinese nation. Let the northwest wind blow my body and tremble, but my bones have not been slackened in the slightest. Let my stomach be so hungry that I灌河water to fill my stomach, but my spirit has not been discouraged in the slightest. I do not expect personal enjoyment. There are so many people in this tragic era who are displaced. From now on, I will enrich my knowledge,鍛鍊my physique, prepare to ride horses and draw bows, and wait for the time when the Chinese nation needs me to sacrifice."

The downfall of the last resort was already predicted, and I am not surprised or sighed. Only the experience of life will not 空負my life in an extraordinary way. I painfully say goodbye to my many colleagues, and finally hope that each of us will work hard.
